# StreamElements Chatbot | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the StreamElements Chatbot documentation. This comprehensive guide will help you harness the full potential of our powerful Twitch chatbot, designed to enhance viewer engagement, automate tasks, and create more interactive streams.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------

The StreamElements Chatbot is a versatile tool that can be customized to fit your streaming needs. From basic commands to complex automated responses, our chatbot can handle a wide range of tasks to improve your stream's interactivity and efficiency.

[🗃️ Getting Started\
-------------------\
\
2 items](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands)

[📄️ Changelog\
-------------\
\
Stay updated with the latest changes and improvements to the StreamElements Chatbot.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog)

[🗃️ Commands\
------------\
\
2 items](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands)

[📄️ Counters\
------------\
\
Learn how to use counters in your Twitch streams to track game deaths, missed shots, or any other event.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters)

[🗃️ Spam Filters\
----------------\
\
6 items](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters)

[🗃️ Modules\
-----------\
\
12 items](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules)

[📄️ Quotes\
----------\
\
Learn how to use the StreamElements Quotes system to save and share memorable moments from your stream with your community.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes)

[📄️ Timers\
----------\
\
Learn how to set up and optimize automated messages using StreamElements Chatbot Timers for enhanced stream engagement.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers)

[📄️ Troubleshooting\
-------------------\
\
Resolve common issues with the StreamElements Chatbot, including non-responsive bot, command errors, and timer issues, with our comprehensive troubleshooting guide.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting)

# StreamElements Patch Notes | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

We're excited to announce that **StreamElements Patch Notes** are on the way! This dedicated space will be your go-to source for all the latest updates, improvements, and new features coming to the StreamElements platform.

This is a test post to verify our RSS feed is working correctly! We're also sharing some real improvements we've made to the chatbot system.

# Archive | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/archive#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

# StreamElements Patch Notes - Coming Soon | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/patch-notes-coming-soon#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

We're excited to announce that **StreamElements Patch Notes** are on the way! This dedicated space will be your go-to source for all the latest updates, improvements, and new features coming to the StreamElements platform.

🎯 What to Expect[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/patch-notes-coming-soon#-what-to-expect "Direct link to 🎯 What to Expect")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once we launch, you'll find:

*   **📊 Feature Updates** - New tools and capabilities to enhance your streaming experience
*   **🔧 Bug Fixes** - Resolutions to reported issues and performance improvements
*   **⚡ Performance Enhancements** - Speed and reliability improvements across all services
*   **🎨 UI/UX Improvements** - Better interface design and user experience updates
*   **🔗 Integration Updates** - New platform integrations and API improvements

📅 Stay Tuned[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/patch-notes-coming-soon#-stay-tuned "Direct link to 📅 Stay Tuned")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We're putting the finishing touches on our patch notes system and will begin publishing regular updates very soon. Make sure to bookmark this page and check back regularly for the latest StreamElements news!

💬 Feedback Welcome[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/patch-notes-coming-soon#-feedback-welcome "Direct link to 💬 Feedback Welcome")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Have suggestions for what you'd like to see in our patch notes? Reach out to us through our usual support channels - we'd love to hear from you!

* * *

**Follow us:** [Discord](https://discord.gg/se)
 • [Twitter](https://twitter.com/StreamElements)
 • [Twitch](https://www.twitch.tv/streamelements)

*   [🎯 What to Expect](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/patch-notes-coming-soon#-what-to-expect)
    
*   [📅 Stay Tuned](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/patch-notes-coming-soon#-stay-tuned)
    
*   [💬 Feedback Welcome](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/patch-notes-coming-soon#-feedback-welcome)

# RSS Feed Test - Chatbot Performance Improvements | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is a test post to verify our RSS feed is working correctly! We're also sharing some real improvements we've made to the chatbot system.

🚀 Performance Enhancements[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#-performance-enhancements "Direct link to 🚀 Performance Enhancements")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Response Time Improvements[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#response-time-improvements "Direct link to Response Time Improvements")

*   **Reduced latency** by 30% for custom commands
*   **Optimized database queries** for point calculations
*   **Improved memory management** during peak chat activity

### Enhanced Stability[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#enhanced-stability "Direct link to Enhanced Stability")

*   **Better error handling** for malformed commands
*   **Automatic retry logic** for failed API calls
*   **Improved connection pooling** for database operations

🐛 Bug Fixes[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#-bug-fixes "Direct link to 🐛 Bug Fixes")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Fixed issue where `!points` command would timeout during large streams
*   Resolved problem with special characters in usernames
*   Corrected timezone handling in `!uptime` command
*   Fixed counter reset bug affecting long-running streams

📡 RSS Feed Testing[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#-rss-feed-testing "Direct link to 📡 RSS Feed Testing")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're reading this in your RSS reader, congratulations! Our feed is working perfectly. You can subscribe to our patch notes at:

**RSS Feed URL:** `https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss.xml`

🔄 What's Next[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#-whats-next "Direct link to 🔄 What's Next")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   More performance optimizations coming next week
*   New moderation features in development
*   Enhanced analytics dashboard updates

* * *

**Questions?** Join our [Discord](https://discord.gg/se)
 or check our [documentation](https://docs.streamelements.com/)
 for more details.

*   [🚀 Performance Enhancements](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#-performance-enhancements)
    *   [Response Time Improvements](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#response-time-improvements)
        
    *   [Enhanced Stability](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#enhanced-stability)
        
*   [🐛 Bug Fixes](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#-bug-fixes)
    
*   [📡 RSS Feed Testing](https://docs.streamelements.com/patch-notes/rss-feed-test#-rss-feed-testing)

[!8ball\

Use the !uptime command in StreamElements chatbot to check the current stream's duration.

[!when\

----](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot)

Manage your StreamElements chatbot with the !bot command. Control bot behavior, including muting, unmuting, and removing the bot from chat.

[!cancelraffle\
-------------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle)

Immediately cancel an active raffle on your channel using the StreamElements chatbot !cancelraffle command.

[!closestore\
-----------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore)

Learn how to use the !closestore command in StreamElements chatbot to quickly disable all regular (non-SFX) items in your loyalty store.

[!command\
--------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command)

Manage StreamElements chatbot custom commands directly from chat using the !command (!cmd) functions: add, remove, edit, alias, show, options.

[!disablesfx\
-----------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx)

Learn how to use the !disablesfx command in StreamElements chatbot to quickly disable all sound effect (SFX) items in your loyalty store.

[!editcounter\
------------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter)

Learn how to use the !editcounter command in StreamElements chatbot to set, increment, or decrement custom counter values directly from chat.

[!enablesfx\
----------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/enablesfx)

Learn how to use the !enablesfx command in StreamElements chatbot to quickly re-enable all sound effect (SFX) items in your loyalty store.

[!filesay\
--------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/filesay)

Use the !filesay command in StreamElements chatbot to send multiple lines of text from a URL to chat, ideal for bulk commands like bans.

[!hypecup\
--------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/hypecup)

Use the !hypecup command in StreamElements chatbot to clear the HypeCup overlay contribution list on your Twitch stream.

[!level\
------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/level)

Learn how moderators can use the !level command in StreamElements chatbot to view and manually override user permission levels.

[!module\
-------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/module)

Use the !module command in StreamElements chatbot to enable or disable specific chatbot modules (like games, points, etc.) directly from chat.

[!nuke\
-----](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/nuke)

Use the !nuke command in StreamElements chatbot to moderate chat by timing out, banning, or deleting recent messages matching specific text or regex.

[!nukeusername\
-------------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/nukeusername)

Use the !nukeusername command in StreamElements chatbot to moderate chat by timing out or banning users whose usernames match specific text or regex.

[!openstore\
----------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/openstore)

Learn how to use the !openstore command in StreamElements chatbot to quickly re-enable all regular (non-SFX) items in your loyalty store.

[!pause\
------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/pause)

Use the !pause command in StreamElements chatbot to temporarily stop the media request playback without clearing the queue.

[!permit\
-------](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit)

Use the !permit command in StreamElements chatbot to temporarily allow a specific user to post links in chat without being timed out.

[!play\
-----](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play)

Use the !play (!resume, !unpause) command in StreamElements chatbot to resume paused media request playback.

[!queue\

# Changelog | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

8 August 2024[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#8-august-2024 "Direct link to 8 August 2024")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 🆕 New Features[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-new-features "Direct link to 🆕 New Features")

*   Added new variable: [`$(teamfighttactics)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/teamfighttactics)
    

### 🛞 Improvements[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-improvements "Direct link to 🛞 Improvements")

*   Fixed an issue which caused some [Viewer Queue](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue)
     commands to send multiple responses

6 August 2024[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#6-august-2024 "Direct link to 6 August 2024")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 🆕 New Features[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-new-features-1 "Direct link to 🆕 New Features")

*   Added support for Twitch Warnings in spam filters and banned words
*   Introduced a new dropdown menu for customizable moderation actions:
    *   Warn and delete message
    *   Timeout user
    *   Ban user
    *   Delete message only

29 July 2024[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#29-july-2024 "Direct link to 29 July 2024")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 🛞 Improvements[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-improvements-1 "Direct link to 🛞 Improvements")

*   Fixed an issue with [Link Protection](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/links)
     which could flag emote combinations as links on YouTube

25 July 2024[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#25-july-2024 "Direct link to 25 July 2024")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 🛞 Improvements[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-improvements-2 "Direct link to 🛞 Improvements")

*   Enhanced loyalty system for more dynamic point and watchtime distribution:
    *   For partner channels: Points and watchtime now awarded at intervals between 1-10 minutes
    *   For non-partner channels: Points and watchtime now awarded at intervals between 5-10 minutes
    *   This replaces the previous fixed 10-minute interval for all channels

24 July 2024[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#24-july-2024 "Direct link to 24 July 2024")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 📚 Documentation[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-documentation "Direct link to 📚 Documentation")

*   Updated existing documentation for clarity and accuracy
*   Comprehensive documentation update for all [default commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default)
     and [variables](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables)
    
*   Enhanced documentation for [`$(channel)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/channel)
    , including previously missing arguments
*   Improved documentation for [`$(user)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user)
     & [`$(sender)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/sender)
     variables

*   [8 August 2024](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#8-august-2024)
    *   [🆕 New Features](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-new-features)
        
    *   [🛞 Improvements](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-improvements)
        
*   [6 August 2024](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#6-august-2024)
    *   [🆕 New Features](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#-new-features-1)
        
*   [29 July 2024](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/changelog#29-july-2024)

# StreamElements Chatbot Commands | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

StreamElements offers a comprehensive set of chatbot commands to elevate your streaming experience. Our command system is designed to provide both out-of-the-box functionality and customizable options, ensuring that streamers of all levels can create engaging and interactive chat environments.

Default Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands#default-commands "Direct link to Default Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our platform includes a diverse array of pre-configured commands that are ready to use immediately. These default commands cover a wide spectrum of functionalities, including:

*   Moderation tools
*   Viewer engagement features
*   Stream information queries
*   Game-specific interactions

You can utilize these commands as-is or tailor them to align with your unique streaming style and community needs.

Custom Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands#custom-commands "Direct link to Custom Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to our default offerings, StreamElements empowers you to create bespoke commands tailored specifically to your channel and community. Custom commands open up a world of possibilities, allowing you to:

*   Design unique viewer interactions
*   Implement channel-specific features
*   Create personalized responses and actions
*   Develop commands that complement your content and brand

With custom commands, you can craft a truly distinctive chat experience that sets your stream apart and fosters a stronger connection with your audience.

Explore our documentation to learn how to leverage both default and custom commands to maximize engagement and streamline your streaming workflow.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands#overview)
    
*   [Default Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands#default-commands)
    
*   [Custom Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands#custom-commands)

---

# Custom Commands | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

In addition to the default commands, you can also create your own custom commands. Custom commands allow you to create commands that are tailored to your channel and your community. You can use custom commands to create unique interactions and functionalities that are not possible with the default commands.

Managing Custom Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#managing-custom-commands "Direct link to Managing Custom Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 2 ways to manage a custom commands:

1.  Through the creator dashboard
2.  Directly in chat with the [!command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command)
     command

### Using the Dashboard to manage custom commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#using-the-dashboard-to-manage-custom-commands "Direct link to Using the Dashboard to manage custom commands")

See [Creating a command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands)
 in `Getting Started`

### Using chat to manage Custom Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#using-chat-to-manage-custom-commands "Direct link to Using chat to manage Custom Commands")

#### Creating a Custom Command in chat[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#creating-a-custom-command-in-chat "Direct link to Creating a Custom Command in chat")

The general Syntax is the following:

    !command add <command name> <response>

#### Modifying a Custom Command in chat[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#modifying-a-custom-command-in-chat "Direct link to Modifying a Custom Command in chat")

    !command edit <command name> <response>

#### Deleting a Custom Command in chat[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#deleting-a-custom-command-in-chat "Direct link to Deleting a Custom Command in chat")

    !command remove <command name>

#### Displaying the commands text in chat[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#displaying-the-commands-text-in-chat "Direct link to Displaying the commands text in chat")

    !command show <command name>

##### Example Output[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#example-output "Direct link to Example Output")

    @Styler, command test: ${channel} This is a test command. ${settitle ${1:}}

#### Changing the options / permissions / cooldowns of a command[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#changing-the-options--permissions--cooldowns-of-a-command "Direct link to Changing the options / permissions / cooldowns of a command")

    !command options <command name> <-option> <value>

For specifics read the documentation for the [!command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command)
 command

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Dynamic Greeting Command[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#dynamic-greeting-command "Direct link to Dynamic Greeting Command")

This command greets the user and tells them when they last visited the stream.

    !cmd add !hello $(user), welcome to the stream! You last visited $(user.lastseen) ago.

**Output:**

    Viewer: !helloBot: Viewer123, welcome to the stream! You last visited 2 days 5 hours ago.

Variables used:

*   [$(user)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#user)
     - The name of the viewer
*   [$(user.lastseen)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlastseen)
     - The time the viewer last visited the stream

### Stream Uptime Command[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#stream-uptime-command "Direct link to Stream Uptime Command")

This command shows how long the stream has been live, the current game, and viewer count.

    !cmd add !stream The stream has been live for $(uptime). We're currently playing $(channel.game) for $(channel.viewers) viewers!

**Output:**

    Viewer: !streamBot: The stream has been live for 2 days 5 hours. We're currently playing Fortnite for 1234 viewers!

Variables used:

*   [$(uptime)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/channel#channeluptime)
     - The time the stream has been live
*   [$(channel.game)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/channel#channelgame)
     - The game the stream is currently playing
*   [$(channel.viewers)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/channel#channelviewers)
     - The number of viewers currently watching the stream

### Weather Command[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#weather-command "Direct link to Weather Command")

This command checks the weather for a specified location.

    !cmd add !weather ${sender}, weather in: $(weather ${1:})

**Output:**

    Viewer: !weather TokyoBot: Styler, weather in: Aarhus, Denmark: 🌜 17.7 °C (63.9 °F). Feels like 17.7 °C (63.9 °F). Patchy rain nearby. Wind is blowing from the South at 9.7 km/h (6.0 mp/h). 89% humidity. Visibility: 10 km (6 miles). Air pressure: 1008 hPa.

Variables used:

*   [$(weather)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/weather)
     - The current weather in a specified location

### Shoutout Command[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#shoutout-command "Direct link to Shoutout Command")

This command sends a simple shoutout to a specified user.

    !cmd add !shoutout Check out ${1}, they are playing ${game ${1}} at https://twitch.tv/${1}

**Output:**

    Viewer: !shoutout StylerBot: Check out Styler, they are playing Counter-Strike at https://twitch.tv/Styler

Variables used:

*   [$(args)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/args)
     - The name of the user to shoutout
*   [$(game)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/game)
     - The game the user is currently playing

*   [Managing Custom Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#managing-custom-commands)
    *   [Using the Dashboard to manage custom commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#using-the-dashboard-to-manage-custom-commands)
        
    *   [Using chat to manage Custom Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#using-chat-to-manage-custom-commands)
        
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#examples)
    *   [Dynamic Greeting Command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#dynamic-greeting-command)
        
    *   [Stream Uptime Command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#stream-uptime-command)
        
    *   [Weather Command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#weather-command)
        
    *   [Shoutout Command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/custom#shoutout-command)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Default commands are pre-configured chat commands available in the StreamElements Chatbot. These commands provide essential functionality for streamers, moderators, and viewers to interact with the chat and manage the stream.

List of Default Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default#list-of-default-commands "Direct link to List of Default Commands")

Below is a list of commonly used default commands. Click on each command to learn more about its usage, parameters, and configuration options.

[📄️ !8ball\
----------\
\
Ask the StreamElements chatbot a question with the !8ball command and receive a random, magic 8-ball style answer. Fun for viewer engagement.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/8ball)

-----------\

---------------\

--------------\

Learn how moderators can manually add loyalty points to viewers using the StreamElements !addpoints chatbot command. Manage your community rewards.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints)

-----------\
\

--------\

# !8ball | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/8ball#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/8ball#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!8ball` command simulates a magic 8-ball toy, providing random responses to viewer questions. This interactive feature engages your audience and adds an element of unpredictability to your chat.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/8ball#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the command, type `!8ball` followed by an optional question in the chat. The chatbot will respond with a random fortune-like answer.

    !8ball [question]

_The `[question]` part is entirely optional and does not influence the random outcome._

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/8ball#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!8ball Will I win my next game?

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:It is decidedly so.

example chat

ViewerName:!8ball What should I have for dinner?

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Cannot predict now.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/8ball#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!8ball` command is part of the **8ball module**.

*   **Module Status:** Ensure the 8ball module is enabled in your StreamElements dashboard under `Chatbot` -> `Modules`.
*   **Custom Responses:** You can customize the list of possible responses the command uses within the module settings on your dashboard.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/8ball#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following aliases can be used interchangeably with `!8ball`:

*   `!eightball`
*   `!69ball`
*   `!420ball`

# !accept Command | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!accept` command allows users to accept pending duel requests initiated by the [`!duel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel)
 command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the `!accept` command, simply type it in the chat when you have a pending duel request.

    !accept

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

Challenger:!duel TargetUser 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@TargetUser, @Challenger wants to duel you for 10 points, you can !accept or !deny within 2 minutes

TargetUser:!accept

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:TargetUser won the Duel vs Challenger PogChamp

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This command does not take any parameters.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!accept` command is part of the **Duel module**. This module must be enabled in your StreamElements chatbot settings under `Chatbot` -> `Modules` for the command to function.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!duel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel)
    : Initiate a duel with another user.
*   [`!cancelduel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel)
    : Cancel an outgoing duel request.
*   [`!deny`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny)
    : Deny an incoming duel request.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept#overview)

# Counters | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Counters are an easy way to keep track of certain things in your stream. They can be used to keep track of how many times you've died in a game, or how many times you've missed a cannon minion in league of legends.

You can manage your counters in the [StreamElements Dashboard](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/counters)
 or use the variable directly from chat listed below.

Variables[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#variables "Direct link to Variables")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `getcount` - Retrieves the current count of the counter. For more information, refer to the [getcount documentation](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/getcount)
    .
*   `count` Increments or decrements the counter. For more information, refer to the [count documentation](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/count)
    .

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Add counter command[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#add-counter-command "Direct link to Add counter command")

Let's start by adding a new counter command for missed cannons in league of legends:

1.  Create a new command by typing `!cmd add cannon ${count cannon}`
2.  Now when you type `!cannon` in chat, it will increment the counter by 1.

![Image](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/0-5d2ebdc88bda06ddd0b922362682e4fa.png "Add counter command")

* * *

### Get the current count[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#get-the-current-count "Direct link to Get the current count")

Let's create another command to see how many cannons you've missed (Without incrementing the counter):

1.  Create a new command by typing `!cmd add missedcannons ${getcount cannon}`
2.  Now when you type `!missedcannons` in chat, it will show you the current count of the cannon counter.

![Image](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/1-7d2e94c639f86ccb4b833badaaf79c76.png "Get the current count")

*   [Variables](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#variables)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#examples)
    *   [Add counter command](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#add-counter-command)
        
    *   [Get the current count](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/counters#get-the-current-count)

---

# Banned Words Filter | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/bannedwords#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

The Banned Words filter is a tool that helps maintain the chat environment by removing messages that contain banned phrases and patterns. This filter is highly customizable and supports the creation of multiple groups, each with its own set of banned phrases.

These phrases can be simple text or they can be regular expressions (regexp), providing a high degree of flexibility in defining what constitutes a banned phrase. For example, you could ban a specific word, or use a regular expression to ban any word that contains a certain sequence of characters.

To use this filter, simply define your groups and their associated banned phrases or patterns. Any incoming message that matches a banned phrase or pattern in any group will be automatically removed.

To create a group, click the **Add Group** button. This will create a new group with the default name **Group 1**.

### Example[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/bannedwords#example "Direct link to Example")

![Example](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/preview-a0bca01b5581d9a83fd907e964030951.png)

*   [Example](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/bannedwords#example)

# Getting Started with Commands | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Commands are the main way users will interact with the bot in your chat. They can be used to trigger actions, or to display information to your users. In this example we will create a command that will display the amount of time that has past since a user was last seen in chat.

Step 1 - Open the command creation tool[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#step-1---open-the-command-creation-tool "Direct link to Step 1 - Open the command creation tool")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From the [bot command dashboard](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/commands)
    , navigate to the "Custom Commands" tab.
2.  Click the "Add New Command" button to open the command creation tool.

![Step 1](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/step_1-52d360a86042ce7df3b1f4fefb2bada6.png "Step 1")

Step 2 - Basic settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#step-2---basic-settings "Direct link to Step 2 - Basic settings")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enter the desired name for your new command. For this example we will name the command "lastseen".
    
2.  Optional: In the "Response Type" dropdown, select the method you would like the bot to use to send the response.
    

*   "Say" will send the response as a chat message as it is entered in the basic settings.
*   "Mention" will send the response as a chat message, but will prefix the message with [`@$(user),`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/sender)
    .
*   "Reply" will send the response as a native reply to the user who triggered the command.
    *   NOTE: If the platform does not support native replies, the response will be sent as a "Mention" instead.
*   "Whisper" will send the response as a whisper to the user who triggered the command.

3.  Add your desired response. For a list of all available variables, see the [variables documentation](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables)
    .

![Step 2](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/step_2-64d5fb2c26172448dffc46af21d96c48.png "Step 2")

Step 3 - Advanced settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#step-3---advanced-settings "Direct link to Step 3 - Advanced settings")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Optional: Add one or more command aliases to allow users to trigger the same command using alternate names.
2.  Click the "Activate Command" button to save your new command.

![Step 3](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/step_3-7c3e76aa1456315acc282ca4dc2c4723.png "Step 3")

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#overview)
    
*   [Step 1 - Open the command creation tool](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#step-1---open-the-command-creation-tool)
    
*   [Step 2 - Basic settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#step-2---basic-settings)
    
*   [Step 3 - Advanced settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/commands#step-3---advanced-settings)

---

# Emote Filter | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/emotes#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

The Emote filter helps manage the use of emotes in chat messages. It checks the number of emotes in a message and compares them with the set limit. If a message violates this limit, the filter takes action according to the configured settings.

### Supported Settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/emotes#supported-settings "Direct link to Supported Settings")

*   `Timeout duration`: This is the duration (in seconds) for which a user will be timed out if their message violates the emote limit.
*   `Excluded user groups`: These are the user groups that are exempt from the emote filter. Messages from users in these groups will not be checked by the filter.
*   `Custom timeout message`: This is the message that will be displayed when a user is timed out due to a violation of the emote limit. This message can be customized to provide specific information about the violation and the timeout.
*   `Maximum amount`: This is the maximum number of emotes allowed in a message. If a message contains more emotes than this limit, it will be flagged by the filter.

*   [Supported Settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/emotes#supported-settings)

---

# Spam Filters | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters#overview "Direct link to Overview")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Spam filters are essential tools for maintaining a clean and enjoyable chat environment during your streams. StreamElements Chatbot offers various types of filters to help you automatically moderate messages and protect your chat from unwanted content.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters#usage "Direct link to Usage")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use spam filters, you need to enable and configure them in your StreamElements dashboard. Once set up, the filters will automatically scan incoming messages and take action based on your settings.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To configure spam filters:

1.  Log in to your StreamElements dashboard
2.  Navigate to the Chatbot section
3.  Select "Spam Filters" from the menu
4.  Choose the filter type you want to set up
5.  Adjust the settings according to your preferences
6.  Save your changes

# Caps Filter | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/caps#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

The Caps filter helps manage the use of capital letters in chat messages. It checks the number and percentage of capital letters in a message and compares them with the set limits. If a message violates these limits, the filter takes action according to the configured settings.

### Supported Settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/caps#supported-settings "Direct link to Supported Settings")

*   `Timeout duration`: This is the duration (in seconds) for which a user will be timed out if their message violates the capital letters limits.
*   `Excluded user groups`: These are the user groups that are exempt from the caps filter. Messages from users in these groups will not be checked by the filter.
*   `Custom timeout message`: This is the message that will be displayed when a user is timed out due to a violation of the capital letters limits. This message can be customized to provide specific information about the violation and the timeout.
*   `Maximum amount`: This is the maximum number of capital letters allowed in a message. If a message contains more capital letters than this limit, it will be flagged by the filter.
*   `Minimum characters`: This is the minimum number of characters a message must have before the filter checks for a violation. If a message contains fewer characters than this limit, it will not be checked by the filter.
*   `Maximum percent`: This is the maximum percentage of a message that can be capital letters. If the percentage of capital letters in a message exceeds this limit, it will be flagged by the filter.

*   [Supported Settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/caps#supported-settings)

---

# Symbol Filter | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/symbol#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

The Symbol filter helps manage the use of symbols in chat messages. It checks the number and percentage of symbols in a message and compares them with the set limits. If a message violates these limits, the filter takes action according to the configured settings.

### Supported Settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/symbol#supported-settings "Direct link to Supported Settings")

*   `Maximum amount`: This is the maximum number of symbols allowed in a message. If a message contains more symbols than this limit, it will be flagged by the filter.
*   `Minimum amount`: This is the minimum number of symbols a message must have before the filter checks for a violation. If a message contains fewer symbols than this limit, it will not be checked by the filter.
*   `Maximum percent`: This is the maximum percentage of a message that can be symbols. If the percentage of symbols in a message exceeds this limit, it will be flagged by the filter.
*   `Timeout duration`: This is the duration (in seconds) for which a user will be timed out if their message violates the symbol limits.
*   `Excluded user groups`: These are the user groups that are exempt from the symbol filter. Messages from users in these groups will not be checked by the filter.
*   `Custom timeout message`: This is the message that will be displayed when a user is timed out due to a violation of the symbol limits. This message can be customized to provide specific information about the violation and the timeout.

*   [Supported Settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/symbol#supported-settings)

# Getting Started with Timers | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Timers allow you to automatically post announcements, social links, schedules, or any other messages at regular intervals in your chat. This guide will help you set up and manage timers using the StreamElements chatbot.

Step 1 - Access the Bot Timers Dashboard[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-1---access-the-bot-timers-dashboard "Direct link to Step 1 - Access the Bot Timers Dashboard")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Navigate to your StreamElements dashboard.
2.  Go to the Bot section and select "Timers".

Step 2 - Create a New Timer[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-2---create-a-new-timer "Direct link to Step 2 - Create a New Timer")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Click the "ADD NEW TIMER" button in the top right corner.
2.  In the expanded timer settings, enter a name for your timer in the "Timer name" field.

Step 3 - Configure Timer Settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-3---configure-timer-settings "Direct link to Step 3 - Configure Timer Settings")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Message**: Enter the message you want the timer to post in the "Enter a message" field.
    
2.  **Intervals**:
    
    *   Set the "Online interval" in minutes. This is how often the timer will post when your stream is live.
    *   Set the "Offline interval" in minutes. This determines how often the timer will post when you're not streaming.
3.  **Chat Lines**: Specify the minimum number of chat lines required in the last 5 minutes to activate the timer. This prevents the timer from posting in an inactive chat.
    
4.  **Stream Title Keywords** (Optional):
    
    *   Enter keywords that, when present in your stream title, will enable the timer.
5.  **Stream Categories** (Optional):
    
    *   Enter categories that, when selected for your stream, will enable the timer.
6.  **Response Messages** (Optional):
    
    *   Add multiple messages that the timer will cycle through by clicking "+ ADD MESSAGE".

Step 4 - Activate the Timer[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-4---activate-the-timer "Direct link to Step 4 - Activate the Timer")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Once you've configured all settings, click the "ACTIVATE TIMER" button at the bottom of the timer settings.
    
2.  The timer will now appear in your list of active timers, where you can easily enable/disable it using the toggle switch.
    

Step 5 - Managing Timers[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-5---managing-timers "Direct link to Step 5 - Managing Timers")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   To edit an existing timer, click the pencil icon next to the timer in the list.
*   To delete a timer, click the trash can icon.
*   Use the search bar at the top to quickly find specific timers.

Tips for Effective Timer Use[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#tips-for-effective-timer-use "Direct link to Tips for Effective Timer Use")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Keep messages concise and relevant to your audience.
*   Use timers sparingly to avoid spamming your chat.
*   Utilize the chat lines feature to ensure timers only post during active periods.
*   Consider using different intervals for online and offline states to match chat activity levels.

Remember, timers are a powerful tool for maintaining engagement and sharing information, but overuse can be disruptive to your chat experience. Balance is key!

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#overview)
    
*   [Step 1 - Access the Bot Timers Dashboard](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-1---access-the-bot-timers-dashboard)
    
*   [Step 2 - Create a New Timer](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-2---create-a-new-timer)
    
*   [Step 3 - Configure Timer Settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-3---configure-timer-settings)
    
*   [Step 4 - Activate the Timer](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-4---activate-the-timer)
    
*   [Step 5 - Managing Timers](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#step-5---managing-timers)
    
*   [Tips for Effective Timer Use](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/gettingstarted/timers#tips-for-effective-timer-use)

---

# Troubleshooting | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

This section aims to help you quickly resolve common issues you might encounter with the StreamElements Chatbot and answer frequently asked questions.

Troubleshooting[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#troubleshooting-1 "Direct link to Troubleshooting")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Chatbot Not Responding[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#chatbot-not-responding "Direct link to Chatbot Not Responding")

*   **Check if the bot is currently active in your channel.** You can do this by going to your StreamElements dashboard and ensuring the bot is turned on.
*   **Ensure the bot is not banned or ignored in your channel.** Sometimes, the bot might have been accidentally banned, which would prevent it from posting messages.

### Commands Not Working[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#commands-not-working "Direct link to Commands Not Working")

*   **Verify the command syntax.** Ensure that the command is typed correctly, including the prefix (usually `!`).
*   **Check command settings.** Some commands may be set to work only for moderators or the streamer. You can adjust these settings in your StreamElements dashboard.
*   **Command cooldown.** If a command was recently used, it might be on cooldown. Check the command's settings to see if there's a cooldown period set.

### Timers Not Triggering[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#timers-not-triggering "Direct link to Timers Not Triggering")

*   **Check the timer settings.** Ensure the timers are enabled and configured with the correct intervals and chat lines required to trigger.
*   **Insufficient chat activity.** Some timers require a minimum amount of chat activity to trigger. Encourage your viewers to be more active in chat.

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### How do I add the StreamElements Chatbot to my channel?[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#how-do-i-add-the-streamelements-chatbot-to-my-channel "Direct link to How do I add the StreamElements Chatbot to my channel?")

To add the chatbot to your channel, go to your StreamElements dashboard, navigate to the Chatbot section, and follow the instructions for adding the bot to your channel.

### Can I create custom commands?[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#can-i-create-custom-commands "Direct link to Can I create custom commands?")

Yes, you can create custom commands through the StreamElements dashboard under the "Commands" section. Here, you can define the command name, response, and other settings like cooldowns and user level restrictions.

### How do I set up moderation filters?[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#how-do-i-set-up-moderation-filters "Direct link to How do I set up moderation filters?")

Moderation filters can be set up in the StreamElements dashboard under the "Spam Filters" section. You can configure filters for links, caps, symbols, and more to keep your chat clean and safe.

### Can the chatbot respond to commands with custom messages?[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#can-the-chatbot-respond-to-commands-with-custom-messages "Direct link to Can the chatbot respond to commands with custom messages?")

Yes, the chatbot can respond to commands with custom messages that you define. You can set these messages when creating or editing a command in your StreamElements dashboard.

### How do I remove the chatbot from my channel?[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#how-do-i-remove-the-chatbot-from-my-channel "Direct link to How do I remove the chatbot from my channel?")

If you wish to remove the chatbot from your channel, you can do so by going to the Chatbot section in your StreamElements dashboard and selecting the option to part the bot from your channel.

* * *

If your issue isn't listed here or if you have more questions, please visit our [Discord](https://discord.gg/se)
 or contact our Support Team for further assistance.

*   [Troubleshooting](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/troubleshooting#troubleshooting-1)

# Link Filter | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/links#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

The Link filter helps manage the posting of links in chat messages. It checks if a message contains any links and compares them with the set allowlist and blocklist. If a message contains a link that is not in the allowlist or is in the blocklist, the filter takes action according to the configured settings.

### Supported Settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/links#supported-settings "Direct link to Supported Settings")

*   `Timeout duration`: This is the duration (in seconds) for which a user will be timed out if their message violates the link rules. Setting to 0 will just delete the message.
*   `Excluded user groups`: These are the user groups that are exempt from the link filter. Messages from users in these groups will not be checked by the filter.
*   `Custom timeout message`: This is the message that will be displayed when a user is timed out due to a violation of the link rules. This message can be customized to provide specific information about the violation and the timeout.
*   `Allowlist`: This is a list of links or link patterns that are allowed in messages. The filter supports wildcard characters in this list, allowing for flexible rules.
*   `Blocklist`: This is a list of links or link patterns that are not allowed in messages. Any link that matches a pattern in this list is treated as harmful and will result in a harsher punishment for the user.

*   [Supported Settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/links#supported-settings)

---

# Paragraph Filter | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/paragraph#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

The Paragraph filter helps manage the length of chat messages. It checks the number of characters in a message and compares them with the set limit. If a message violates this limit, the filter takes action according to the configured settings.

### Supported Settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/paragraph#supported-settings "Direct link to Supported Settings")

*   `Maximum amount`: This is the maximum number of characters allowed in a message. If a message contains more characters than this limit, it will be flagged by the filter.
*   `Timeout duration`: This is the duration (in seconds) for which a user will be timed out if their message violates the character limit.
*   `Excluded user groups`: These are the user groups that are exempt from the paragraph filter. Messages from users in these groups will not be checked by the filter.
*   `Custom timeout message`: This is the message that will be displayed when a user is timed out due to a violation of the character limit. This message can be customized to provide specific information about the violation and the timeout.

*   [Supported Settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/filters/paragraph#supported-settings)

---

# !alerts | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!alerts` command allows streamers and moderators to dynamically manage StreamElements overlay alerts during a live broadcast. This tool helps control alert playback directly from chat for actions like muting, skipping, or pausing.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To manage overlay alerts, use the `!alerts` command followed by the desired action.

    !alerts <action>

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!alerts mute

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Successfully muted alerts

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!alerts skip

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Successfully skipped alerts

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!alerts pause

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Successfully paused alerts

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<action>` (Required): The action to perform on the alerts. Valid actions are:
    *   `mute`: Turns off alert sounds.
    *   `unmute`: Turns alert sounds back on.
    *   `skip`: Skips the currently playing alert.
    *   `pause`: Pauses the alert queue; currently playing alerts will finish.
    *   `unpause`: Resumes the alert queue.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command controls alerts within your StreamElements overlays. Ensure your overlays are active.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/alerts#configuration)

# Chatbot Timers | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Chatbot timers are automated messages or actions that occur at specified intervals during a live stream. They serve to remind viewers about certain aspects of the stream, such as rules or upcoming events, and can also be used to automatically execute commands at regular intervals.

### Settings[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers#settings "Direct link to Settings")

#### Messages[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers#messages "Direct link to Messages")

Each timer can be configured with multiple messages, which will be cycled through each time the timer is activated. Timers can be set to run both while live and offline, or can be configured to run only in one of these states.

#### Interval[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers#interval "Direct link to Interval")

The frequency of each timer can be set in minutes, determining how often it will be activated. Additionally, a minimum amount of chat lines that must be sent in the interval for the timer to be activated can be set, ensuring the timer only runs when chat activity is high enough.

#### Chat lines[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers#chat-lines "Direct link to Chat lines")

The minimum number of chat messages that must be sent before a timer can be executed. This allows you to prevent timers from spamming the chat when there is less chatroom activity.

#### Conditions (new)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers#conditions-new "Direct link to Conditions (new)")

Timers can now be configured with specific conditions. This allows a timer to be activated only when a particular condition is fulfilled. For instance, a timer can be set to run exclusively when the stream is categorized under "Just Chatting", or if the stream title includes a specific keyword.

You can find your timers here: [Dashboard](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/timers)

*   [Settings](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/timers#settings)

---

# !accountage Command | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!accountage` command allows users to check the creation date (age) of a Twitch account. This tool is particularly useful for moderators to verify user authenticity or determine eligibility for certain privileges based on account age.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the command, type `!accountage` followed by an optional username. If no username is provided, it checks the account age of the user running the command.

    !accountage [username]

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!accountage StreamElements

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@ModUser, StreamElements was created 10 years 2 months 28 days 7 hours ago.

example chat

ViewerBob:!accountage

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@ViewerBob, your account was created 3 years 5 months 12 days 4 hours ago.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `[username]` (Optional): The Twitch username of the account you want to check. If omitted, the command checks the account age of the user who issued the command.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This command requires a connection to Twitch to fetch the account creation date. Ensure your StreamElements bot account is properly linked to Twitch.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!accountage` command has the following default aliases:

*   `!accage`
*   `!created`

These aliases can be used interchangeably with the main command.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!followage`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/followage)
    : Checks how long a user has been following the channel.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accountage#examples)

# Quotes | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

The Quotes system allows you and your moderators to save memorable moments, funny sayings, or notable events from your streams. Viewers can then recall these quotes using chat commands, creating a fun way to relive past highlights with your community.

You can manage your quotes in the [StreamElements Dashboard](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/quotes)
.

Dashboard Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#dashboard-overview "Direct link to Dashboard Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Bot Quotes page provides a centralized location to manage all your saved quotes:

*   **Search**: Filter quotes by text content
*   **Add Quote**: Manually add new quotes via the dashboard
*   **Quote List**: View all quotes with their ID, text, creation date, associated game, and who added them
*   **Actions**: Edit or delete individual quotes

Adding Quotes[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#adding-quotes "Direct link to Adding Quotes")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Via Chat[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#via-chat "Direct link to Via Chat")

Moderators and the broadcaster can add quotes directly from chat using the `!quote add` command:

    !quote add Never gonna give you up!

The bot will confirm the quote was added and assign it a unique ID.

### Via Dashboard[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#via-dashboard "Direct link to Via Dashboard")

1.  Navigate to [Bot Quotes](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/quotes)
     in your dashboard
2.  Click the **\+ ADD QUOTE** button
3.  Enter the quote text
4.  Click **Save**

The quote will be saved with the current timestamp.

Displaying Quotes[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#displaying-quotes "Direct link to Displaying Quotes")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Random Quote[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#random-quote "Direct link to Random Quote")

Viewers can display a random quote from your collection:

    !quote

### Specific Quote[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#specific-quote "Direct link to Specific Quote")

To display a specific quote by its ID:

    !quote 42

Managing Quotes[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#managing-quotes "Direct link to Managing Quotes")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Editing Quotes[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#editing-quotes "Direct link to Editing Quotes")

To edit an existing quote:

1.  Go to the [Bot Quotes](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/quotes)
     page
2.  Find the quote you want to edit
3.  Click the pencil icon in the Actions column
4.  Update the quote text
5.  Save your changes

### Removing Quotes[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#removing-quotes "Direct link to Removing Quotes")

**Via Chat (Moderator+):**

    !quote remove 42

**Via Dashboard:**

1.  Find the quote in the list
2.  Click the trash icon in the Actions column
3.  Confirm the deletion

Chat Command Reference[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#chat-command-reference "Direct link to Chat Command Reference")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Command | Description | Permission |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `!quote` | Display a random quote | Everyone |
| `!quote <id>` | Display a specific quote | Everyone |
| `!quote add <text>` | Add a new quote | Moderator+ |
| `!quote remove <id>` | Remove a quote | Moderator+ |

### Command Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#command-aliases "Direct link to Command Aliases")

*   `!quote add` can also be written as `!quote +`
*   `!quote remove` can also be written as `!quote -`

Quote Variables[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#quote-variables "Direct link to Quote Variables")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use quote variables in custom commands and timers. For detailed documentation, see the [$(quote) variable reference](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/quote)
.

*   `$(quote)` - Returns a random quote
*   `$(quote <id>)` - Returns a specific quote by ID

### Example Custom Command[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#example-custom-command "Direct link to Example Custom Command")

Create a command that displays a random quote with custom formatting:

    !cmd add randomquote Here's a memorable moment: $(quote)

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The permission levels for adding and removing quotes can be adjusted under **Chatbot** -> **Chat Commands** -> **Default Commands** in your [StreamElements Dashboard](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/commands/default)
.

*   [Dashboard Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#dashboard-overview)
    
*   [Adding Quotes](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#adding-quotes)
    *   [Via Chat](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#via-chat)
        
    *   [Via Dashboard](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#via-dashboard)
        
*   [Displaying Quotes](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#displaying-quotes)
    *   [Random Quote](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#random-quote)
        
    *   [Specific Quote](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#specific-quote)
        
*   [Managing Quotes](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#managing-quotes)
    *   [Editing Quotes](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#editing-quotes)
        
    *   [Removing Quotes](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#removing-quotes)
        
*   [Chat Command Reference](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#chat-command-reference)
    *   [Command Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/quotes#command-aliases)
