# !addpoints | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!addpoints` command empowers streamers and moderators to manually add points to a specific viewer's balance within the StreamElements loyalty system. This is useful for rewarding viewers for actions outside the standard point triggers, correcting point balances, or running special promotions.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add points to a viewer, use the following syntax in your chat:

    !addpoints <username> <amount>

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<username>` (Required): The exact username of the viewer receiving points.
*   `<amount>` (Required): The number of points (positive integer) to award.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The `!addpoints` command requires the **Loyalty system** to be active. Enable it in your **StreamElements Dashboard** under **Loyalty** -> **Loyalty Settings**.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under **Chatbot** -> **Chat Commands** -> **Default Commands**.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!addpoints StreamFan123 1000

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@BroadcasterName, added 1000 points to StreamFan123. They now have 5961 points.

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser99:!addpoints LoyalViewer 50

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@ModUser99, added 50 points to LoyalViewer. They now have 1280 points.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!setpoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints)
    : Set a user's points to a specific value.
*   [`!givepoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/givepoints)
    : Allow users to give points to each other.
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Check a user's current point balance.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#overview)

*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#configuration)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints#examples)

# 8ball Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The 8ball module is an interactive chat feature that simulates the classic Magic 8 Ball toy. It allows viewers to ask questions and receive random, customizable responses, enhancing engagement and entertainment in your Twitch chat.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the 8ball module, viewers type `!8ball` followed by their question in the chat. The chatbot will then respond with a random answer from a predefined list.

**Syntax:** `!8ball <question>`

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Viewer: `!8ball Will I win my next game?` Chatbot: `The 8ball says: It is certain.`
    
2.  Viewer: `!8ball Should I order pizza tonight?` Chatbot: `The 8ball says: Ask again later.`
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The 8ball command does not have any additional parameters. The question asked by the viewer is optional and does not affect the randomized response.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Streamers and moderators can customize the 8ball responses in the StreamElements dashboard:

1.  Navigate to the Chatbot section
2.  Find the 8ball module in the list of available modules
3.  Click on "Edit" to access the module settings
4.  Modify the list of possible responses
5.  Save your changes

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, there are no aliases for the 8ball command. However, streamers can create custom aliases in the StreamElements dashboard if desired.

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/eightball#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: Can I add my own custom responses to the 8ball?** A: Yes, you can customize the list of possible responses in the module settings of your StreamElements dashboard.

# Emote Combo Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Emote Combo feature is an interactive chat module that encourages viewers to create chains of consecutive emotes. It adds a fun, engaging element to your stream by challenging viewers to maintain and extend emote streaks.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Emote Combo feature activates automatically when viewers start sending consecutive emotes in chat. Here's how it works:

1.  A viewer initiates the combo by sending a message containing a single emote.
2.  Subsequent messages must contain only the same emote to continue the combo.
3.  The combo count increases with each consecutive matching emote.
4.  The combo ends when a different emote or any other message is sent.

Example[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#example "Direct link to Example")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Emote Combo Example](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/emotecombo-5402bb898996264a1ea625d70a096ab8.png)

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Emote Combo feature is typically enabled by default. Streamers can customize the following settings in the StreamElements dashboard:

*   Minimum combo count to display
*   Custom messages for combo milestones

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: Can I use custom emotes for the Emote Combo?** A: Yes, both Twitch global emotes and channel-specific emotes work with the Emote Combo feature.

**Q: Is there a limit to how long a combo can be?** A: No

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#usage)
    
*   [Example](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#example)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#configuration)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotecombo#faq)

# Chat Alerts Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Chat Alerts module is a powerful feature of the StreamElements chatbot that automatically posts messages in your Twitch chat when specific events occur. This helps streamers acknowledge viewer actions, enhance engagement, and keep the community informed about important stream events.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Chat Alerts are triggered automatically when configured events happen during your stream. No manual commands are required to activate them.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Follower Alert:
    
        New follower hype! Welcome to the stream, @NewFollower123! Thanks for joining our community!
    
2.  Subscription Alert:
    
        @Subscriber456 just subscribed for 3 months! Thank you for your continued support!
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Chat Alerts can be customized for various events. Here are some of the key parameters:

*   **Event Type**: The specific action that triggers the alert (e.g., follow, subscription, raid)
*   **Message**: The text that appears in chat when the event occurs
*   **Minimum Threshold**: Optional minimum value for events like donations or bit cheers

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up Chat Alerts:

1.  Access your StreamElements dashboard
2.  Navigate to the Chatbot section
3.  Find the Chat Alerts module
4.  Enable the alerts you want to use
5.  Customize the message and parameters for each alert type

Event Types[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#event-types "Direct link to Event Types")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Chat Alerts can be configured for various events, including:

*   Followers
*   Tips/Donations
*   Ad Breaks
*   Subscriptions
*   Cheers (Bits)
*   Loyalty Point Redemptions
*   Raids
*   Hype Trains
*   Polls
*   Charity Events

Each event type can have its own customized message and trigger conditions.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#configuration)
    
*   [Event Types](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/chatalerts#event-types)

# Emote Pyramid Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Emote Pyramid is an engaging chat game that encourages viewer participation and creates a fun atmosphere in your stream. Players attempt to collaboratively build a pyramid of emotes in the chat, increasing the challenge and excitement as the pyramid grows.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Emote Pyramid game doesn't require any specific commands to start. It begins organically when viewers participate by following these steps:

1.  A viewer initiates the game by sending a single emote in the chat.
2.  Subsequent messages should contain the same emote, with the number of repetitions increasing by one each time.
3.  The game continues until the pyramid is successfully completed or interrupted.

**Note:** The pyramid is considered interrupted if:

*   Another user sends a different message.
*   The same emote is not repeated the correct number of times.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Successful Emote Pyramid[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#successful-emote-pyramid "Direct link to Successful Emote Pyramid")

    Viewer1: PogChampViewer2: PogChamp PogChampViewer3: PogChamp PogChamp PogChampViewer4: PogChamp PogChamp PogChamp PogChampViewer5: PogChamp PogChamp PogChampViewer6: PogChamp PogChampViewer7: PogChampChatbot: nice 4-width Kappa pyramid Styler LUL 

### Interrupted Emote Pyramid[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#interrupted-emote-pyramid "Direct link to Interrupted Emote Pyramid")

    Viewer1: KappaViewer2: Kappa KappaViewer3: Kappa Kappa KappaViewer4: Nice try!Viewer5: Kappa Kappa Kappa Kappa

In this example, the pyramid was interrupted by Viewer4's message.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Emote Pyramid feature doesn't require any specific configuration. It's an organic chat game that relies on viewer participation.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#examples)
    *   [Successful Emote Pyramid](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#successful-emote-pyramid)
        
    *   [Interrupted Emote Pyramid](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#interrupted-emote-pyramid)
        
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emotepyramid#configuration)

# Live Announcement Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Live Announcement module is a feature of the StreamElements Chatbot that automatically posts a message in the chat when a stream goes live. This helps notify viewers that the stream has started and provides essential information about the stream.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When enabled, the Live Announcement module works automatically without any manual input required. As soon as the stream goes live, the chatbot will post a predefined message in the chat.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Default announcement:

    ExampleStreamer is now live! Streaming Fortnite: Late night squad games with friends!

2.  Custom announcement:

    🎉 ExampleStreamer just went live! They're playing Minecraft and the stream title is "Building a mega castle - Day 3". Don't miss out!

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Live Announcement message can include the following parameters:

*   `${channel.display_name}`: The display name of the channel
*   `{title}`: The title of the live stream
*   `{game}`: The game or category being streamed

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To configure the Live Announcement module:

1.  Go to your StreamElements dashboard
2.  Navigate to the Chatbot settings
3.  Find the "Live Announcement" section
4.  Enable the module
5.  Customize the announcement message using the available parameters

Example configuration:

    🔴 ${channel.display_name} is now live! 🎮 Playing {game} 📌 {title}

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: Can I customize the announcement message?** A: Yes, you can customize the message in the StreamElements dashboard using the available parameters.

**Q: How often does the Live Announcement trigger?** A: The announcement triggers once per stream, when the stream initially goes live.

**Q: Can I use custom variables in the announcement?** A: Currently, only the predefined parameters (`${channel.display_name}`, `{title}`, and `{game}`) are supported.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#configuration)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/liveannouncement#faq)

# Duel Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Duel module is an interactive chat game that allows users to challenge each other to a duel, wagering points for a chance to win.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To initiate a duel, use the following command:

    !duel <username> <points>

Replace `<username>` with the name of the user you want to challenge, and `<points>` with the number of points you want to wager.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Challenging a user to a duel for 100 points:
    
        !duel StreamNinja 100
    
2.  Accepting a duel challenge:
    
        !accept
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<username>`: The name of the user you want to challenge.
*   `<points>`: The number of points you want to wager in the duel.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!accept`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept)
    : Accepts a duel challenge.
*   [`!deny`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny)
    : Declines a duel challenge.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can configure the following settings for the Duel module:

| Setting | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Cooldown | The cooldown period between duel challenges. |
| Maximum amount | The maximum number of points that can be wagered in a duel. |

How It Works[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#how-it-works "Direct link to How It Works")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  A user initiates a duel using the `!duel` command.
2.  The challenged user has the option to accept or decline the duel.
3.  If accepted, the game randomly determines a winner.
4.  The winner receives the wagered points.

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: How is the winner determined?** A: The winner is randomly selected by the system when both users have accepted the duel.

**Q: Can I challenge multiple users at once?** A: No, you can only challenge one user at a time.

**Q: What happens if the challenged user doesn't respond?** A: If the challenged user doesn't respond within a set time (usually a few minutes), the duel request expires, and no points are exchanged.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#parameters)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#related-commands)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#configuration)
    
*   [How It Works](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#how-it-works)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/duel#faq)

# Roulette Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Roulette module is an interactive chat game that allows users to wager their points in a roulette-style gamble. It adds excitement and engagement to your stream by giving viewers a chance to win or lose points based on luck.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start a game of roulette, users type the following command in chat:

    !roulette <points>

The module then randomly determines the outcome of the roulette spin. If the user wins, they receive a payout based on their wager. If they lose, they forfeit the points they wagered.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Wager 100 points:
    
        !roulette 100
    
2.  Wager 50% of total points:
    
        !roulette 50%
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<points>`: The number of points to wager. This can be expressed in several ways:
    *   As a whole number (e.g., `100`)
    *   As a percentage of the user's total points (e.g., `50%`)
    *   Using `k` to represent thousands (e.g., `5k` for 5,000 points)
    *   Using `m` to represent millions (e.g., `1m` for 1,000,000 points)

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!roulette`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette)
    : Initiates the roulette game.
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
     - Check your current point balance

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Streamers can configure the Roulette module in the StreamElements dashboard, including:

*   Minimum wager amount
*   Cooldown period between uses
*   How rigged the roulette is

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: Can users go into negative points?** A: No, users can only wager points they currently have.

**Q: Is there a limit to how often someone can use the Roulette command?** A: Yes, there's typically a cooldown period between uses, which can be configured by the streamer.

**Q: Can moderators disable the Roulette game?** A: Yes, moderators with appropriate permissions can enable or disable the Roulette module through the StreamElements dashboard.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#parameters)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#related-commands)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#configuration)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/roulette#faq)

---

# Viewer Queue Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#overview "Direct link to Overview")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Viewer Queue module allows streamers to create and manage a queue where viewers can join and be selected. This feature is particularly useful for organizing viewer interactions, such as game participation, Q&A sessions, or giveaways during live streams.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#usage "Direct link to Usage")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the Viewer Queue module, streamers and moderators can use specific commands to manage the queue, while viewers can join the queue using a designated command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#examples "Direct link to Examples")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Starting a queue for viewers to join a game:

    Streamer: !queue openBot: The queue is now open! Type !join to enter the queue.Viewer1: !joinBot: Viewer1 has joined the queue at position 1.Viewer2: !joinBot: Viewer2 has joined the queue at position 2.

2.  Selecting a viewer from the queue:

    Streamer: !queue nextBot: The next viewer in the queue is Viewer1!

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Viewer Queue module doesn't have specific parameters, but it uses various commands to manage the queue.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!queue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue)
    : The main command for viewers to join the queue.
*   [`!queue open`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue)
    : Opens the queue for viewers to join (mod only).
*   [`!queue close`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue)
    : Closes the queue, preventing new entries (mod only).
*   [`!queue clear`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue)
    : Clears all entries from the queue (mod only).
*   [`!queue next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue)
    : Selects the next viewer from the queue (mod only).
*   [`!queue list`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue)
    : Displays the current queue (mod only).

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Viewer Queue module can be configured in the StreamElements dashboard. Streamers can customize settings such as:

*   Maximum queue size
*   Auto-close queue when full
*   Cooldown between joins
*   Custom messages for queue events

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: Can viewers join the queue multiple times?** A: Viewers can only join the queue once.

**Q: How long does a queue last?** A: The queue remains active until it's manually closed or cleared by a moderator, or until the stream ends.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#parameters)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#related-commands)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#configuration)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/viewerqueue#faq)

---

# Votekick Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Votekick module is a powerful chatbot feature that enables viewers to vote on whether to temporarily remove a user from the chat.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To initiate a votekick, use the following command:

    !votekick <username>

Replace `<username>` with the name of the user you want to start a vote against.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Start a votekick for user "TrollUser123":
    
        !votekick TrollUser123
    
2.  Vote in an active votekick (using default keywords):
    
        PogChamp
    
    or
    
        NotLikeThis
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!votekick` command doesn't require additional parameters beyond the target username.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Customize the Votekick module behavior through the following settings:

| Setting | Description | Options/Range |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Voting Mode | Choose the voting interface | "Twitch Chat" or "Twitch Polls" |
| Minimum Votes | Set the required votes to kick | Minimum: 1 |
| Voting Duration | Set the length of the voting period | 10 to 1800 seconds |
| Kick Duration | Set how long the user is removed from chat | 10 to 1,209,600 seconds |
| Yea Keyword | Set the keyword for a "yes" vote | Recommended: Twitch emote |
| Nay Keyword | Set the keyword for a "no" vote | Recommended: Twitch emote |

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/votekick#configuration)

---

# Bingo Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#overview "Direct link to Overview")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Emote Bingo module is an interactive chat game that generates a bingo card with various emotes. Players compete to identify the correct emote.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#usage "Direct link to Usage")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start a Bingo game, a moderator must use the `!bingo` command with specific parameters. The game ends when a user correctly identifies the chosen emote in chat.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#examples "Direct link to Examples")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Start a game using only Twitch emotes with a 100 point reward:
    
        !bingo twitch 100
    
2.  Start a game using all available emote providers with a 500 point reward:
    
        !bingo all 500
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<emote_provider>`: Specifies the source of emotes for the game. Options include:
    *   `twitch`: Twitch emotes only
    *   `bttv`: BetterTTV emotes only
    *   `ffz`: FrankerFaceZ emotes only
    *   `7tv`: 7TV emotes only
    *   `all`: Includes emotes from all providers
*   `<points>`: The number of points awarded to the winner

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [!bingo](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo)
    

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No additional configuration is required for the Bingo module.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#parameters)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#related-commands)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/emote-bingo#configuration)

# Slotmachine Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#overview "Direct link to Overview")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Slotmachine module is an interactive chat game that allows viewers to wager their points on a virtual slot machine. Players can win or lose points based on the outcome of the spin, adding an element of excitement to the stream chat.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#usage "Direct link to Usage")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start a game, viewers use the `!slots` command followed by the number of points they wish to wager. The slot machine then spins and displays a combination of emotes. If three matching emotes appear, the player wins and receives a payout based on their wager.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#examples "Direct link to Examples")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Wager 100 points:
    
        !slots 100
    
2.  Wager 50% of total points:
    
        !slots 50%
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<points>`: The number of points to wager. This can be expressed in several ways:
    *   As a whole number (e.g., `100`)
    *   As a percentage of the user's total points (e.g., `50%`)
    *   Using `k` to represent thousands (e.g., `5k` for 5,000)
    *   Using `m` to represent millions (e.g., `1m` for 1,000,000)

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!slots`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots)
    : Initiates the slot machine game.
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Check your current point balance

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Streamers can customize the following aspects of the Slotmachine module:

*   Emotes used in the slot machine
*   Minimum wager amount

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#parameters)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#related-commands)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/slotmachine#configuration)

---

# Raffle Module | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Raffle module is an interactive chat game that allows streamers to engage their audience. Moderators can initiate a raffle, and viewers can join for a chance to win. This feature is great for giveaways, selecting participants for games, or simply adding fun interaction to your stream.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  A moderator starts the raffle using `!raffle` or `!sraffle`.
2.  Viewers join the raffle by typing `!join` in chat.
3.  After a set time, the raffle ends, and winner(s) are randomly selected.
4.  The winner(s) are announced in chat.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Single-winner raffle:

    Moderator: !sraffleBot: A raffle has started! Type !join to enter.Viewer1: !joinViewer2: !joinBot: The raffle has ended. The winner is Viewer2!

Multi-winner raffle:

    Moderator: !raffleBot: A multi-winner raffle has started! Type !join to enter.[Multiple viewers join]Bot: The raffle has ended. The winners are Viewer3, Viewer7, and Viewer12!

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `!raffle [points] [duration]`: Start a multi-winner raffle. Optional points and duration in seconds (default is 5000 points and 60 seconds).
*   `!sraffle [points] [duration]`: Start a single-winner raffle. Optional points and duration in seconds (default is 5000 points and 60 seconds).

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!raffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/raffle)
    : Initiates the raffle process.
*   [`!join`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/join)
    : Used by viewers to enter an ongoing raffle.
*   [`!cancelraffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle)
    : Cancels the current raffle (moderators only).

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: How are winners determined in multi-winner raffles?** A: The number of winners scales based on the number of participants:

*   Over 200 participants: 1 winner per 20 entrants
*   51-200 participants: 1 winner per 8 entrants
*   21-50 participants: 1 winner per 5 entrants
*   11-20 participants: 1 winner per 4 entrants
*   2-10 participants: Half the participants win (rounded down)
*   1 participant: That participant wins

**Q: Can I customize the raffle duration?** A: Yes, you can specify the duration in seconds when starting a raffle, e.g., `!raffle 5000 120` for a 5000 point raffle that runs for 2 minutes.

**Q: How do I prevent the same person from winning multiple times?** A: The Raffle module automatically ensures that each participant can only win once per raffle.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#parameters)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#related-commands)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/modules/raffle#faq)

---

# Overlay Editor shortcuts | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/overlay-editor-shortcuts#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

| Key | Action |
| --- | --- |
| Del | Delete selected widget |
| Shift + d | Duplicate selected widget |
| Arrow | Move widget 1px |
| Shift + arrow | Move widget 10px |
| Esc | Unselect widgets |
| Ctrl/Command + z | Undo last action |
| Ctrl/Command + y | Redo last undo action |
| Alt + x | Reset zoom |
| Alt + f | Fit to screen |
| Shift + g | Group selected widgets |
| Shift + u | Ungroup selected widget group |

# !bot | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!bot` command allows streamers and moderators to control the behavior of the StreamElements chatbot during a stream. This command provides essential functions for managing the bot's presence and activity in the chat via several subcommands.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!bot` command uses the following general structure:

    !bot <subcommand>

Permissions

By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use the `!bot` command and its subcommands. The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Subcommands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#subcommands "Direct link to Subcommands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section details the available subcommands for `!bot`.

### mute[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#mute "Direct link to mute")

Temporarily prevents the bot from sending _any_ messages (including commands and timers) in the chat.

**Syntax**

    !bot mute

**Example**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!bot mute

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, I have been muted.

### unmute[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#unmute "Direct link to unmute")

Allows the bot to resume sending messages in the chat after being muted.

**Syntax**

    !bot unmute

**Example**

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!bot unmute

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Broadcaster, I have been unmuted.

### part[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#part "Direct link to part")

Makes the bot leave the chat channel entirely. The bot will need to be invited back manually via the StreamElements dashboard if you wish for it to return.

**Syntax**

    !bot part

**Example**

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!bot part

UnknownUser:StreamElements has left the channel.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!commands`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/commands)
    : Lists all available bot commands.
*   [`!command`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command)
    : Manages custom commands.
*   [`!module`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/module)
    : Enables or disables chatbot modules.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are no default aliases for the `!bot` command or its subcommands.

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **How do I get the bot back after using `!bot part`?** You need to go to your StreamElements dashboard, navigate to the Chatbot settings, and click the button to make the bot join your channel again.
    
*   **Does `!bot mute` stop timers?** Yes, muting the bot prevents it from sending timer messages as well as command responses.
    

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#usage)
    
*   [Subcommands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#subcommands)
    *   [mute](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#mute)
        
    *   [unmute](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#unmute)
        
    *   [part](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#part)
        
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#related-commands)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#aliases)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bot#faq)

---

# !cancelraffle | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!cancelraffle` command allows streamers and moderators to immediately halt any active raffle or giveaway initiated by [`!raffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/raffle)
 or [`!sraffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle)
 on their channel.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To cancel an ongoing raffle, use the following command in chat:

    !cancelraffle

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!cancelraffle

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:The raffle was canceled!

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!cancelraffle

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:There is no active raffle to cancel.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The `!cancelraffle` command requires the **Raffle module** to be active. Enable it in your **StreamElements Dashboard** under `Chatbot` -> `Modules`.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!raffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/raffle)
    : Starts a new raffle where users can enter multiple times (using points).
*   [`!sraffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle)
    : Starts a new raffle where each user can only enter once (using keywords).

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are no default aliases for this command. However, you can create custom aliases in your StreamElements dashboard if desired.

# !bingo | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!bingo` command starts an interactive emote bingo game in your chat. It randomly selects an emote from a specified platform (Twitch, BTTV, FFZ, 7TV), and viewers try to guess the correct emote to win loyalty points.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use this command to start a new bingo game.

    !bingo <platform> <points>

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command to start a game.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!bingo twitch 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Bingo started! Guess the Twitch emote to win 100 points!

viewer1:Kappa

viewer2:LUL

viewer3:PogChamp

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Congratulations viewer3! You guessed the correct emote PogChamp and won 100 points!

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!bingo all 250

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Bingo started! Guess the emote (Twitch, BTTV, FFZ, 7TV) to win 250 points!

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<platform>` (Required): The platform(s) to use for emotes. Valid options:
    *   `twitch`: Twitch global and channel emotes.
    *   `bttv`: BetterTTV emotes.
    *   `ffz`: FrankerFaceZ emotes.
    *   `7tv`: 7TV emotes.
    *   `all`: Includes emotes from all supported platforms.
*   `<points>` (Required): The number of loyalty points to reward the winner.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Ensure the **Bingo module** is enabled in your StreamElements dashboard under `Chatbot` -> `Modules`.
*   A **Loyalty system** must be active. Enable it under `Loyalty` -> `Loyalty Settings`.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.
*   You can customize the bingo game by adjusting the reward amount and using different emote platforms to vary the game's difficulty.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Check a user's current loyalty points balance.
*   [`!top`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top)
    : See the leaderboard for points or watch time.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bingo#related-commands)

# !bet | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!bet` command allows viewers to use their loyalty points to bet on the outcome of a contest or event defined by the streamer. This command is used **while a bet is active**, which is initiated through the StreamElements dashboard or via chatbot commands like [`!contest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest)
.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To place a bet while a betting contest is open, viewers use the following syntax:

    !bet <option> <points>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!bet win 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@ViewerName, you have bet 100 points on Win.

example chat

HighRoller:!bet lose 5k

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@HighRoller, you have bet 5000 points on Lose.

example chat

PercentBetta:!bet optionA 25%

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@PercentBetta, you have bet 750 points on optionA.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<option>` (Required): The specific betting option the viewer wants to choose (defined by the streamer when starting the bet).
*   `<points>` (Required): The number of loyalty points to wager. This can be a specific number, a percentage (`50%`), or use `k` for thousands (`5k`), `m` for millions (`1m`).

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Betting contests are managed via the **Betting module** in the StreamElements dashboard or through commands like [`!contest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest)
    . Streamers define the options, duration, and other settings there.
*   Viewers need sufficient loyalty points to place a bet.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!contest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest)
    : Starts a betting contest (requires Moderator permissions).
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Checks a user's current loyalty point balance.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet#related-commands)

# !cancelduel | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!cancelduel` command allows a user to cancel an **outgoing** duel request they initiated with the [`!duel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel)
 command _before_ the challenged user accepts or denies it.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To cancel your pending outgoing duel request, simply type the command in chat:

    !cancelduel

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

Challenger:!duel TargetUser 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@TargetUser, @Challenger wants to duel you for 10 points, you can !accept or !deny within 2 minutes

Challenger:!cancelduel

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Challenger, Duel request cancelled.

example chat

ViewerName:!cancelduel

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@UserName, You do not have any pending outgoing duel requests.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!cancelduel` command is part of the **Duel module**. This module must be enabled in your StreamElements chatbot settings under `Chatbot` -> `Modules` for the command to function.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!duel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel)
    : Initiate a duel with another user.
*   [`!accept`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept)
    : Accept an incoming duel request.
*   [`!deny`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny)
    : Deny an incoming duel request.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel#examples)

# Getting Started | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

This guide explains how to create a Custom Widget or Custom Code AlertBox using StreamElements' Overlay Editor UI.

We'll start by creating an Overlay, then add widgets like an AlertBox and a Custom Widget, which you can edit.

Creating an Overlay[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#creating-an-overlay "Direct link to Creating an Overlay")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Navigate to the [Overlays](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/overlays)
     section.
2.  Click the **NEW OVERLAY** button.

![New Overlay button](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/new-overlay-button-e0720e8203cfa45f2661d3475222aca4.png)

3.  Choose your resolution and click the **START** button.

tip

Overlay size: Usually it should match your stream's resolution, or be smaller if you'd like to do the repositioning in your broadcasting software.

AlertBox[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#alertbox "Direct link to AlertBox")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The AlertBox is a native widget that displays live events from the queue in a popup-like behavior.

To create an AlertBox:

1.  Click the **+** button in the overlay editor.

![New widget plus button](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/new-widget-plus-button-a8d4f977d2172b18254daa719f8eead1.png)

2.  Select **AlertBox** in the **ALERTS** section.

![New widget alert box](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/new-widget-alert-box-f8e9de59298ac80f5946d3ba1396c8e0.png)

### Enabling Custom Code for AlertBox[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#enabling-custom-code-for-alertbox "Direct link to Enabling Custom Code for AlertBox")

To enable custom code for AlertBox:

1.  Open options for AlertBox.
2.  Go to the "Followers" tab.
3.  Toggle the "Enable custom CSS" option for the alert type you want to use.

Custom Widget[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#custom-widget "Direct link to Custom Widget")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Custom Widget is a native widget that you can use to display any content you want. It's ideal for displaying your own content in the overlay and can consume local events (like tips, follows, etc.) as well as remote events read from a websocket or REST API.

To create a Custom Widget:

1.  Click the **+** button in the overlay editor.

![New widget plus button](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/new-widget-plus-button-a8d4f977d2172b18254daa719f8eead1.png)

2.  Select **Custom Widget** in the **STATIC/CUSTOM** section.

![New widget custom code](https://docs.streamelements.com/assets/images/new-widget-custom-code-27736622f81bdf8ce762a28a864f96ae.png)

*   [Creating an Overlay](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#creating-an-overlay)
    
*   [AlertBox](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#alertbox)
    *   [Enabling Custom Code for AlertBox](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#enabling-custom-code-for-alertbox)
        
*   [Custom Widget](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started#custom-widget)
