# Custom Code in Alertboxes | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Before Starting[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#before-starting "Direct link to Before Starting")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Prerequisites[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#prerequisites "Direct link to Prerequisites")

This article requires you to have an Overlay created with an AlertBox with "Custom CSS" enabled. To do so, follow the steps in the [Before Starting](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started)
 article.

Custom Code Editor[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#custom-code-editor "Direct link to Custom Code Editor")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Custom Code Editor is a powerful tool that allows you to write custom code in the Overlay Editor. For more information about the Custom Code Editor, please refer to the [Events](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget-events)
 article.

Inline Variables available[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#inline-variables-available "Direct link to Inline Variables available")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Variable | Description | Example (context or output) |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{{name}}` | Person who is in subject of event. | `{{name}} just followed stream!` |
| `{{amount}}` | Amount if event supports it - amount of bits, months (as resub, can be replaced with (`{{months}}`)), viewers (when hosted, raided). | `{{name}} just cheered with 1000 bits!` |
| `{{tier}}` | Sub tier (sub events only) | `{{name}} subscribed for {{amount}} months at tier {{tier}}` |
| `{{announcement}}` | Message specified in "alert message" box to event. Alias: `{{messageTemplate}}` | `{{announcement}} => {{name}} is our sub for {{amount}}` |
| `{{items}}` | List of items in Merch event | `{{name}} just bought {{items}}` |
| `{{message}}` | HTML user message attached to event (sub, cheer, tip). Remember to provide proper styling for `.alertbox-message-emote` class (alias: `{{userMessage}}`) | `{{message}} =><span class="cheermote-1"><img class="alertbox-message-emote" alt="cheer1" src="https://d3aqoihi2n8ty8.cloudfront.net/actions/cheer/dark/animated/1/2.gif"/>1</span> Hi!` |
| `{{messageRaw}}` | Plain text user message attached to event (sub, cheer, tip). | `{{messageRaw}} => Hi Kappa!` |
| `{{sender}}` | If an action is a sub, `{{sender}}` is replaced with a person who gave it. | `{{sender}} just gifted a sub for {{name}}` |
| `{{currency}}` | Currency if event is a donation. | `{{name}} just tipped us {{currency}} {{amount}} !` |
| `{{image}}` | URL of image attached to alert. | `<img src="{{image}}"/>` |
| `{{video}}` | URL of video attached to alert. | `<video id="video" playsinline autoplay muted style="width:100%; height:100%"><source id="webm" src="{{video}}" type="video/webm"></video>` |
| `{{videoVolume}}` | Video volume (from 0 to 1). If alerts are muted in activity feed this value is set to 0. | `{{videoVolume}} => 0.5` |
| `{{audio}}` | URL of audio attached to alert. | `<audio id="audio" playsinline autoplay ><source id="alertsound" src="{{audio}}" type="audio/ogg"></audio>` |
| `{{audioVolume}}` | Audio volume (from 0 to 1). If alerts are muted in activity feed this value is set to 0. | `{{audioVolume}} => 0.5` |
| `{{widgetDuration}}` | Widget duration in seconds, so you can create exit animation timed perfectly like on examples below: | `{{widgetDuration}} => 5` |

### Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#examples "Direct link to Examples")

#### HTML[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#html "Direct link to HTML")

    <div class="alertbox-message">    <div class="alertbox-message-text">        <span class="alertbox-message-name">{{name}}</span>        <span class="alertbox-message-announcement">{{announcement}}</span>    </div>    <div class="alertbox-message-message">{{message}}</div>

#### JS[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#js "Direct link to JS")

    const hideAfter=parseInt("{widgetDuration}")-1000;const playHideAnimation=()=>{  timeline.reverse(); //or any other thing that will make your alert fancy exit}setTimeout(playHideAnimation,hideAfter);

#### CSS:[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#css "Direct link to CSS:")

    #alertbox {  animation: hide forwards 1s;  animation-delay: calc({widgetDuration}s - 1s);}

*   [Before Starting](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#before-starting)
    *   [Prerequisites](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#prerequisites)
        
*   [Custom Code Editor](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#custom-code-editor)
    
*   [Inline Variables available](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#inline-variables-available)
    *   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-code-alertboxes#examples)

# Websockets | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Astro Websocket Gateway[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#astro-websocket-gateway "Direct link to Astro Websocket Gateway")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Astro is StreamElements' dedicated websocket gateway. It employs a publish-subscribe (pubsub) pattern to facilitate real-time data updates.

### Connection[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#connection "Direct link to Connection")

Connect to the WebSocket endpoint:

    wss://astro.streamelements.com/

If reconnecting after a graceful shutdown, include the reconnect token as a query parameter:

    wss://astro.streamelements.com/?reconnect_token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIs...

If the server is draining, it rejects new connections with **502 Bad Gateway**.

If the connection rate limit is exceeded, it responds with **429 Too Many Requests** and a `Retry-After: 2` header.

### Welcome Message[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#welcome-message "Direct link to Welcome Message")

Immediately after connecting, the server sends a `welcome` message:

    {  "id": "01J5KXYZ...",  "ts": "2026-03-19T12:00:00Z",  "type": "welcome",  "data": {    "message": "You are in a maze of dank memes, all alike.",    "client_id": "01J5KXYZ..."  }}

### Heartbeat[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#heartbeat "Direct link to Heartbeat")

The server sends WebSocket `PING` frames every **30 seconds**. The client must respond with `PONG`. If the server receives no pong within **70 seconds**, it closes the connection.

These are WebSocket control frames, not application-level JSON messages. Most WebSocket libraries handle pong responses automatically.

### Client-to-Server Request[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#client-to-server-request "Direct link to Client-to-Server Request")

The following parameters are used in a client-to-server request:

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `type` | `string` | Defines the type of request. Valid options are `subscribe` and `unsubscribe`. |
| `nonce` | `string` | A unique identifier for the request. Echoed back in the response (optional). |
| `data.topic` | `string` | The topic to subscribe to (required). |
| `data.room` | `string` | The room/channel to subscribe to. Defaults to `""` (global). For `unsubscribe`, if omitted or empty, unsubscribes from all rooms for the topic. |
| `data.token` | `string` | The token used to authenticate the request (required for `subscribe`). |
| `data.token_type` | `string` | Specifies the type of token. Valid options are `jwt`, `oauth2`, and `apikey`. |

Only text frames are accepted. Binary frames are ignored.

Here is an example of a subscribe request:

    {  "type": "subscribe",  "nonce": "req-001",  "data": {    "topic": "channel.activities",    "room": "603abc123",    "token": "eyJhbGc...",    "token_type": "jwt"  }}

Here is an example of an unsubscribe request:

    {  "type": "unsubscribe",  "nonce": "req-002",  "data": {    "topic": "channel.activities",    "room": "603abc123"  }}

To unsubscribe from all rooms for a topic, omit or send an empty `room`:

    {  "type": "unsubscribe",  "nonce": "req-003",  "data": {    "topic": "channel.activities"  }}

### Server-to-Client Messages[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#server-to-client-messages "Direct link to Server-to-Client Messages")

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `id` | `string` | Unique message identifier (ULID). |
| `ts` | `string` | Timestamp in RFC 3339 format. |
| `type` | `string` | Message type: `welcome`, `response`, `message`, or `reconnect`. |
| `topic` | `string` | Present on `message` type. The topic the message was published to. |
| `room` | `string` | Present on `message` type. The room the message was published to. |
| `nonce` | `string` | Present on `response` type. Echoes the nonce from the original request. |
| `error` | `string` | Present on `response` type when an error occurred. |
| `data` | `object` | The message payload. |

Here is an example of a successful subscribe response:

    {  "id": "01J5KXYZ...",  "ts": "2026-03-19T12:00:01Z",  "type": "response",  "nonce": "req-001",  "data": {    "message": "successfully subscribed to topic",    "topic": "channel.activities",    "room": "603abc123"  }}

note

The `room` in the response is the canonical room ID returned by the authorization service, which may differ from the requested value.

### Receiving Messages[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#receiving-messages "Direct link to Receiving Messages")

When a message is published to a topic the client is subscribed to:

    {  "id": "01J5M2AB...",  "ts": "2026-03-19T12:05:00Z",  "type": "message",  "topic": "channel.activities",  "room": "603abc123",  "data": {    "type": "follow",    "provider": "twitch",    "channel": "603abc123"  }}

The `data` field contains the payload from the publisher. See individual [topic pages](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets/topics)
 for payload details.

### Error Codes[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#error-codes "Direct link to Error Codes")

All errors are returned as `response` messages:

    {  "id": "01J5KXYZ...",  "ts": "2026-03-19T12:00:01Z",  "type": "response",  "nonce": "req-001",  "error": "err_bad_request",  "data": {    "message": "human readable description"  }}

| Error | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `err_internal_error` | Server-side failure. |
| `err_bad_request` | Malformed request, missing fields, limit exceeded, or invalid topic. |
| `err_unauthorized` | Authentication failed or permission denied. |
| `err_deadline_exceeded` | Authorization timed out. Retry the request. |
| `rate_limit_exceeded` | Command rate limit exceeded. |
| `invalid_message_type` | Unknown command type (not `subscribe` or `unsubscribe`). |

### Connection Lifecycle[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#connection-lifecycle "Direct link to Connection Lifecycle")

### Reconnection[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#reconnection "Direct link to Reconnection")

Astro supports zero-downtime reconnection during graceful server shutdown.

1.  The server sends a `reconnect` message to each client:

    {  "type": "reconnect",  "data": {    "message": "The server is shutting down.",    "reconnect_token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIs..."  }}

2.  The client saves the `reconnect_token` and opens a new connection:

    wss://astro.streamelements.com/?reconnect_token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIs...

3.  The new server verifies the token and restores all subscriptions automatically — no need to re-subscribe.
    
4.  The client receives a `welcome` message and resumes normal operation.
    

Invalid, expired, or tampered reconnect tokens cause the new connection to be closed immediately.

Available Topics[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#available-topics "Direct link to Available Topics")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For a complete list of available topics and their detailed descriptions, see the [Topics](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets/topics)
 page.

Code Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#code-examples "Direct link to Code Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For implementation examples in different programming languages, see the [Code Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets/examples)
 page.

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q: Why are the messages not coming through? I received the message `successfully subscribed to topic`!**

A: Make sure you're using the token for the specific platform from which you want to receive activities. If you have multiple accounts linked (Twitch, YouTube, Kick, etc.), switch to the correct account on the StreamElements dashboard (click your avatar in the top-right corner) and copy the token again.

**Q: I'm not receiving YouTube activities, and I'm using the correct token.**

A: If your stream is set to `private` or `unlisted`, StreamElements cannot access it. Only public YouTube livestreams are supported.

**Q: How can I make sure I copied the correct token?**

A: If you are using either a JWT or an Overlay Token (apikey), go to the StreamElements dashboard, click your avatar in the top-right corner > select your channel name, and choose the correct channel. After that, you can copy the correct token.

*   [Astro Websocket Gateway](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#astro-websocket-gateway)
    *   [Connection](https://docs.streamelements.com/websockets#connection)

# Code Editor | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

This section describes the StreamElements Custom Code Editor and Widget's Structure. Custom code editor is a simple text editor that allows you to write code, styling, field definitions.

HTML[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#html "Direct link to HTML")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use any HTML tags possible, you can even import external JS if you feel such need. For example if you want to have `$("#selector").toggle('explode');` from jQueryUI, just add

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jqueryui/1.12.1/jquery-ui.js"></script>

And if you want to use Google font in your CSS, just call them by:

    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Chelsea+Market" rel="stylesheet">

This also can be done within CSS Field by importing stylesheet

    @import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Chelsea+Market');

CSS[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#css "Direct link to CSS")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use regular CSS syntax - including animations, transitions

JS[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#js "Direct link to JS")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use pure JavaScript or include external libraries/frameworks to ease your work, however everything will be running in protected sandbox, so you won’t be able to access cookies, `console.*` methods or IndexedDB storage.

FIELDS[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#fields "Direct link to FIELDS")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can create custom variables, so end user doesn't have to interact with code, those fields will be displayed under “OPEN EDITOR” in left panel.

This data can be also called by `{{variableName}}` or `{variableName}` within HTML/CSS/JS code (however for better readibility we suggest using those calls only in HTML/CSS). To access it via JS, you can do it via `onWidgetLoad` listener:

    window.addEventListener('onWidgetLoad', (obj) => {  fieldData = obj.detail.fieldData;  console.log(fieldData) // Show the fields object in the browser console})

At this point we support most of HTML5 input types (except of file - use library inputs such as `video-input` instead), as well as a handful of custom inputs: `colorpicker`, `image-input`, `sound-input`, `video-input`, `googleFont`, `dropdown`, and `slider`.

Adding an invalid type will default it to `"type":"text"`.

There are some reserved field names (all future reserved words will start with `widget`):

*   `widgetName` - Used to set the display name of the widget
*   `widgetAuthor` - Set the author name of the widget (adds a "(by Author)" to the widget name)
*   `widgetDuration` - maximum event queue hold time (seconds) - for Custom Widget (as alertboxes have their own timers). Explained in [resumeQueue section](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#resumequeue-method-and-widgetduration-property)
    

### Example[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#example "Direct link to Example")

#### JSON[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#json "Direct link to JSON")

    {  "someText": {    "type": "text",    "label": "Some Text",    "value": "Default text"  },  "someCheckbox": {    "type": "checkbox",    "label": "Some checkbox",    "value": true,  },  "someColorPicker": {    "type": "colorpicker",    "label": "Some color",    "value": "#0000FF"  },  "someNumber": {    "type": "number",    "label": "Count",    "value": 10,    "min": 0,    "max": 100,    "step": 1  },  "someSlider": {    "type": "slider",    "label": "Counter",    "value": 10,    "min": 0,    "max": 100,    "step": 1  },  "someDropdown": {    "type": "dropdown",    "label": "Choose an option:",    "value": "blue",    "options": {      "blue": "Blue thing",      "apple": "Some apple",      "7": "Lucky number"    }  },  "someImage": {     "type": "image-input",     "label": "Some Image"   }, "someVideo": {   "type": "video-input",   "label": "Some Video" }, "someSound": {   "type": "sound-input",   "label": "Some Audio" },  "fontName": {      "type": "googleFont",      "label": "Select a font:",      "value": "Roboto"    },  "someButton": {    "type": "button",    "label": "Click me!",    "value": "Thanks"  },  "widgetName": {    "type": "hidden",    "value": "My Custom Widget"  },  "widgetDuration": {      "type": "hidden",      "value": 15    }}

Fields of type `image-input`, `video-input`, `sound-input` may use additional parameter `"multiple":true` which allows end user to provide multiple media files within single field. Output will result in array of urls.

If you want to group some fields into a collapsible menu in the left panel, you can add to them the same parameter `"group": "Some group name"`.

#### Local font[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#local-font "Direct link to Local font")

You can use a local font installed on your computer.

    {  "customFont": {    "label": "Custom Font Name",    "type": "text",    "value": "Comic Sans MS"  }}

And add it to your CSS

    * {  font-family: {{customFont}};}

OBS: Restart the browser if you have just installed the font.

#### Input on left panel construction[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#input-on-left-panel-construction "Direct link to Input on left panel construction")

Input field on left panel will look like:

    <input type="TYPE_FROM_JSON" name="FIELD_NAME" value="USER_VALUE_OR_DEFAULT_VALUE"/>

or for dropdown (based on example above)

    <select name="someDropdown">    <option value="blue" selected>Blue thing</option>    <option value="apple">Some apple</option>    <option value="7">Lucky number</option></select>

#### Usage example[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#usage-example "Direct link to Usage example")

Result of those custom fields can be used like:

##### HTML[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#html-1 "Direct link to HTML")

    <div class="message">{{someDropdown}} is an option for today!<span id="additional">{{someText}}</span></div>

##### CSS[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#css-1 "Direct link to CSS")

    .message {    font-size:{{someSlider}}px;    color: {{someColorPicker}};}

##### JS[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#js-1 "Direct link to JS")

    let someVariable,magicNumber;window.addEventListener('onWidgetLoad', function (obj) {    const {fieldData} = obj.detail;    someVariable = fieldData["someText"];    // OR    magicNumber = fieldData.someNumber;    // OR use internal templating variables    magicNumber = parseFloat("{{someNumber}}");});

*   [HTML](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#html)
    
*   [CSS](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#css)
    
*   [JS](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#js)
    
*   [FIELDS](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#fields)
    *   [Example](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure#example)

# !closestore | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!closestore` command allows streamers and moderators to quickly disable all **regular** (non-sound effect) items in the StreamElements loyalty store. This is useful for temporarily preventing viewers from redeeming items while making updates or during specific stream segments.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To disable all regular store items, use the following command in chat:

    !closestore

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!closestore

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully updated 15 items.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!openstore`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/openstore)
    : Re-enables all regular items in the loyalty store.
*   [`!disablesfx`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx)
    : Disables only sound effect (SFX) items in the loyalty store.
*   [`!enablesfx`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/enablesfx)
    : Enables only sound effect (SFX) items in the loyalty store.
*   [`!redeem`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem)
    : Allows viewers to redeem store items.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#examples)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore#configuration)

# Custom Widget & SE_API | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

This is the most powerful tool in SE Overlay editor. You can do a lot of things within this widget using HTML/CSS/JavaScript and accessing variables

**Note:**

> You cannot access `document.cookie` nor `IndexedDB` via it (security reasons), so you need to keep your data elsewhere (accessible via HTTP API) or [SE\_API](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#se_api)
>  store.

Before Starting[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#before-starting "Direct link to Before Starting")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Prerequisites[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#prerequisites "Direct link to Prerequisites")

This article requires you to have an Overlay created with a Custom Widget added there. To do so, follow the steps in the [Before Starting](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/getting-started)
 article.

### Custom Code Editor[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#custom-code-editor "Direct link to Custom Code Editor")

The Custom Code Editor is a powerful tool that allows you to write custom code in the Overlay Editor. For more information about the Custom Code Editor, please refer to the [Widget Structure](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/widget-structure)
 article.

SE\_API[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#se_api "Direct link to SE_API")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SE\_API is a set of functions that provide access to various personalized features for custom widgets. You can check the ones available below:

*   **.store** - A key-value store where objects can be saved globally in a permanent way. The stored data is accessible to other custom widgets under the same account.
    
*   **.cheerFilter** - Removes cheer emotes from a message.
    
*   **.counters** - Retrieves the value of a specific counter.
    
*   **.getOverlayStatus** - Gets the status of the overlay.
    
*   **.resumeQueue** - Resumes the queue immediately.
    
*   **.sanitize** - Sanitizes a message by removing bad words.
    
*   **.setField** - Sets a value for `fieldData[key]`. This does not save the value and works only in the Overlay Editor.
    

### store.set[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#storeset "Direct link to store.set")

Stores an object in the database under the specified keyName (`keyName` can be any alphanumeric string).

**Note 1**: Setting a value will completely overwrite any existing data stored under the same key. Ensure you send the full object, as partial updates are not supported.

**Note 2**: Keys cannot be removed once created. You can update their values as often as needed, but deletion is not possible so far.

    const object = { "item1":"value1", "item2":"value2" }SE_API.store.set("keyName", object);

It emits an `onEventReceived` event for every custom widget. Example payload:

    {  "detail": {    "listener": "kvstore:update",    "event": {      "data": {        "key": "customWidget.keyName",        "value": {          "item1": "value1",          "item2": "value2"        }      }    }  }}

### .store.get[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#storeget "Direct link to .store.get")

Retrieves the contents stored under the specified "keyName" key. The returned obj is the full object stored in the database.

    SE_API.store.get('keyName').then(obj => {  console.log(obj);  /*  The result would look like below:  {   "item1": "value1",   "item2": "value2"  }  */});

### .counters.get[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#countersget "Direct link to .counters.get")

Gets the value of a counter. Your counters can be found at [https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/counters](https://streamelements.com/dashboard/bot/counters)

For example, if you have a counter named "test" with a value of "15":

    SE_API.counters.get('test').then(counter => {  console.log(counter);    /*  The result would look like below:    {    "id": "test",    "count":15  }  */});

### .sanitize[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#sanitize "Direct link to .sanitize")

Sanitizes a message by filtering vulgar words.

For example, if the word "vulgarWord" is marked as a bad word (configured in Tipping Settings) and the filter is set to "Replace bad words with emotes":

    const vulgarSentence = "This is a sentence with vulgarWord";SE_API.sanitize({ message: vulgarSentence }).then(sanityResult => {  console.log(sanityResult);  /*  The result would look like this:  {    "skip": false, // Indicates whether the message should be skipped according to the rules.    "result":{      "message":"This is a sentence with 4Head" // Message after filtering    }      }  */  });

### .cheerFilter[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#cheerfilter "Direct link to .cheerFilter")

Clears cheer emotes from message.

    const message = "shamrock100 This is a cheer message cheer100 cheer100 cheerwhal100"SE_API.cheerFilter(message).then(cheerResult => {  console.log(cheerResult);    /*  The result would look like below:  This is a cheer message  */});

### .getOverlayStatus[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#getoverlaystatus "Direct link to .getOverlayStatus")

Gets overlay Status.

    SE_API.getOverlayStatus().then(status => {  console.log(status);    /*  Result would look like below:  {    "isEditorMode":true,    "muted":false  }  */});

### .setField[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#setfield "Direct link to .setField")

Sets a value for `fieldData[key]`. It works only in the Overlay Editor itself and does not save the value. The third parameter is an optional boolean that indicates whether the overlay should be reloaded after the value is set. The default is true.

    SE_API.setField('key', 'value', false);

### resumeQueue method and widgetDuration property[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#resumequeue-method-and-widgetduration-property "Direct link to resumeQueue method and widgetDuration property")

The `widgetDuration` property defines the maximum event queue hold time (execution time of widget) by widget in seconds (default is 0). For example, if you want to show animations by this widget and don’t want them to overlap, instead of building your own queue, you can use this. This property is defined in JSON (as mentioned above). Premature queue resume can be called by `SE_API.resumeQueue();`

The best way to explain this is through an example:

**Scenario:**

> We have an animation for community sub gifts (only), and we want to use it. The animation duration is dynamic between 7 and 15 seconds, and we don’t want it to overlap on alerts.

**Code:**

#### Fields:[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#fields "Direct link to Fields:")

    {    "widgetDuration":{      "type": "hidden",      "value": 15    }}

#### JS:[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#js "Direct link to JS:")

    let skippable=["bot:counter","event","event:test","event:skip","alertService:toggleSound","message","delete-message","delete-messages","kvstore:update"]; //Array of events coming to widget that are not queued so they can come even if queue is on holdlet playAnimation=(event)=>{    $("container").html(`<div id="sender">${event.sender}</div><div class="amount">${event.amount} subs!</div>`)    return Math.floor(Math.random()*8)+7;};window.addEventListener('onEventReceived', function (obj) {    const listener = obj.detail.listener;  	console.log(obj.detail);    const data = obj.detail.event;	console.log(`RECEIVED ${listener}`);  	if (skippable.indexOf(listener)!==-1) return;  	if (listener !== 'subscriber-latest') {    	console.log("Resuming as event is not sub");        SE_API.resumeQueue();         return;    }  	if (data.bulkGifted !== true && !data.gifted) {    	console.log("Resuming as event is not sub gift");        SE_API.resumeQueue();        return;    }        if (data.name === data.sender) {        console.log("Getting animation duration for premature resume");        let time=playAnimation(data);        setTimeout(SE_API.resumeQueue, time*1000);     }});

*   [Before Starting](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#before-starting)
    *   [Prerequisites](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#prerequisites)
        
    *   [Custom Code Editor](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#custom-code-editor)
        
*   [SE\_API](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#se_api)
    *   [store.set](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#storeset)
        
    *   [.store.get](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#storeget)
        
    *   [.counters.get](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#countersget)
        
    *   [.sanitize](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#sanitize)
        
    *   [.cheerFilter](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#cheerfilter)
        
    *   [.getOverlayStatus](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#getoverlaystatus)
        
    *   [.setField](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#setfield)
        
    *   [resumeQueue method and widgetDuration property](https://docs.streamelements.com/overlays/custom-widget#resumequeue-method-and-widgetduration-property)

---

# !contest | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!contest` command allows anyone in chat to quickly check the status and details of the currently active **betting contest**. It displays the contest question, the available betting options, and the remaining time to place bets.

**Note:** This command _checks_ the status of an active contest. To _start_ a new betting contest, moderators must use the **StreamElements Dashboard**.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To check the active contest details, simply type the command in chat:

    !contest

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!contest

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, the current contest is "Will I clutch this round?". You can !bet for yes, no. Betting ends in 3 mins 15 secs

example chat

ViewerName:!contest

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, there is no active contest.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The `!contest` command requires the **Betting module** to be active. Enable and configure it in your **StreamElements Dashboard** under `Chatbot` -> `Modules`.
*   The command response reflects the settings of the currently active contest (question, options, duration) configured by the streamer/moderator via the dashboard.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!bet`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet)
    : Used by viewers to place bets on the active contest.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/contest#examples)

# !deny | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!deny` command allows a user to reject an **incoming** duel request initiated by another user with the [`!duel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel)
 command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To reject a pending incoming duel request, type the command in chat:

    !deny

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

Challenger:!duel TargetUser 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@TargetUser, @Challenger wants to duel you for 10 points, you can !accept or !deny within 2 minutes

TargetUser:!deny

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@TargetUser denied the duel request from @Challenger.

example chat

ViewerName:!deny

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@UserName, You do not have any pending incoming duel requests to deny.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!deny` command is part of the **Duel module**. This module must be enabled in your StreamElements chatbot settings under `Chatbot` -> `Modules` for the command to function.

    : Initiate a duel with another user.

    : Accept an incoming duel request.
*   [`!cancelduel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel)
    : Cancel an _outgoing_ duel request you initiated.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# !disablesfx | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!disablesfx` command allows streamers and moderators to quickly disable all **sound effect** (SFX) items in the StreamElements loyalty store. This is useful for temporarily preventing viewers from redeeming SFX during specific stream segments or when managing audio.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To disable all SFX store items, use the following command in chat:

    !disablesfx

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!disablesfx

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully updated 5 items.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The `!disablesfx` command requires the **Stream Store** module to be active and configured with SFX items. Manage this in your **StreamElements Dashboard** under `Loyalty` -> `Stream Store`.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!enablesfx`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/enablesfx)
    : Re-enables all sound effect (SFX) items in the loyalty store.
*   [`!closestore`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore)
    : Disables all _regular_ (non-SFX) items in the loyalty store.
*   [`!openstore`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/openstore)
    : Enables all _regular_ (non-SFX) items in the loyalty store.
*   [`!redeem`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem)
    : Allows viewers to redeem store items.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#examples)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx#related-commands)

# !command | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!command` (aliased as `!cmd`) command suite allows streamers and moderators with the appropriate permissions to manage custom chat commands directly from the chat interface. It provides subcommands to add, remove, edit, view aliases, show details, and configure advanced options for any custom command.

Permissions

By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use the `!command` subcommands.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The general syntax follows this pattern:

    !command <subcommand> [arguments...]

Or using the alias:

    !cmd <subcommand> [arguments...]

Replace `<subcommand>` with one of the functions listed below and `[arguments...]` with the required parameters for that specific subcommand.

Subcommands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#subcommands "Direct link to Subcommands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are the available subcommands for `!command`:

### add[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#add "Direct link to add")

Creates a new custom command.

**Syntax:**

    !command add !*command_name* *response_text*

**Example:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!command add !socials Follow me on Twitter @MyHandle!

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully added command !socials.

### remove[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#remove "Direct link to remove")

Deletes an existing custom command.

**Syntax:**

    !command remove !*command_name*

**Example:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!command remove !socials

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully removed command !socials.

### edit[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#edit "Direct link to edit")

Changes the response text of an existing custom command.

**Syntax:**

    !command edit !*command_name* *new_response_text*

**Example:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!command edit !socials Check out my links: example.com/links

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully updated command !socials.

### alias[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#alias "Direct link to alias")

Shows the aliases associated with a specific command.

Note

Aliases themselves can only be created or managed through the StreamElements Dashboard, not via chat commands.

**Syntax:**

    !command alias !*command_name*

**Example:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!command alias !socials

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, Command !socials has aliases: !links, !connect

### show[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#show "Direct link to show")

Displays the full response text and configuration details (level, cost, cooldowns) of a command.

**Syntax:**

    !command show !*command_name*

**Example:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!command show !socials

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, Command !socials: Check out my links: example.com/links (Level: Everyone, Cost: 0, Cooldown: 5s, User Cooldown: 15s)

### options[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#options "Direct link to options")

Configures advanced settings like cooldowns, cost, permission level, response type, enabled status, and usage count for a command. See the [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#parameters-for-options-subcommand)
 section below for details on the available options.

**Syntax:**

    !command options !*command_name* *option1* *value1* [*option2*] [*value2*] ...

_Note: Replace `option1`, `value1`, etc., with the specific parameter flags and values listed in the Parameters section below. You can specify multiple options._

**Example (setting multiple options):**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!command options !socials -cd 10 -usercd 30 -cost 50 -level moderator

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully updated command !socials.

Parameters (for `options` subcommand)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#parameters-for-options-subcommand "Direct link to parameters-for-options-subcommand")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When using the `!command options` subcommand, you specify settings using flags followed by their values. You can set multiple options in a single message. These parameters allow fine-grained control over a command's behavior:

| Parameter | Description | Accepted Values | Example Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `-cd` | Sets the **global command cooldown** (minimum time between _any_ use of the command). | `<seconds>` (e.g., `10`) | `-cd 10` |
| `-usercd` | Sets the **user-specific cooldown** (minimum time the _same user_ must wait before using the command again). | `<seconds>` (e.g., `30`) | `-usercd 30` |
| `-cost` | Sets the **loyalty points cost**. Requires the StreamElements [Loyalty System](https://docs.streamelements.com/docs/loyalty/overview)<br> active. | `<points>` (e.g., `50`) | `-cost 50` |
| `-level` | Sets the **minimum user permission level** required. | `everyone`, `subscriber`, `regular`, `moderator`, `supermoderator`, `broadcaster` | `-level moderator` |
| `-type` | Sets **how the bot responds**. Platform support for `reply` and `whisper` may vary. | `say` (default), `reply`, `whisper` | `-type whisper` |
| `-enable` | Enables the command. | N/A | `-enable` |
| `-disable` | Disables the command, preventing anyone from using it. | N/A | `-disable` |
| `-count` | **Manually sets the command's usage counter**, useful for resetting or adjusting the value used by [`$(count)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/count)<br>. | `<number>` (e.g., `0`) | `-count 0` |

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **`!command`:** `!cmd`
*   **`remove`:** `delete`, `del`, `rem`
*   **`edit`:** `update`
*   **`alias`:** `aliases`
*   **`show`:** `debug`
*   **`options`:** `option`, `opt`, `opts`, `o`, `🔧`

Related Commands and Variables[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#related-commands-and-variables "Direct link to Related Commands and Variables")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!commands`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/commands)
    : Lists available commands.
*   [`$(count)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/count)
    : Variable to display the usage count of a command.
*   [`$(user)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user)
    : Variable representing the user executing the command.
*   [`$(channel)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/channel)
    : Variable representing the channel name.
*   See the full list of [Chatbot Variables](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables)
    .

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **What's the difference between global cooldown (`-cd`) and user cooldown (`-usercd`)?** Global cooldown (`-cd`) applies to _everyone_ – once the command is used, no one can use it again until the cooldown expires. User cooldown (`-usercd`) applies only to the _individual user_ – they have to wait, but other users can still use the command if the global cooldown has passed.
    
*   **How do I reset a command's usage counter?** Use the `options` subcommand with the `-count` parameter: `!command options !<command_name> -count 0`
    
*   **Can I make a command respond with a whisper instead of a public message?** Yes, use the `options` subcommand with the `-type` parameter: `!command options !<command_name> -type whisper`. Note that whisper functionality depends on the chat platform.
    
*   **Why can't I add or edit command aliases using the `!command` system?** Alias management (creating, deleting, editing aliases for commands) is currently only available through the Command page on your StreamElements Dashboard.
    
*   **I'm a moderator, but `!command add` isn't working. Why?** Double-check that the `!command` default command itself hasn't been disabled or had its permission level changed from the default (Moderator). You can check its settings in the `Default Commands` section of your StreamElements Dashboard.
    

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#usage)
    
*   [Subcommands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#subcommands)
    *   [add](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#add)
        
    *   [remove](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#remove)
        
    *   [edit](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#edit)
        
    *   [alias](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#alias)
        
    *   [show](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#show)
        
    *   [options](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#options)
        
*   [Parameters (for `options` subcommand)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#parameters-for-options-subcommand)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#aliases)
    
*   [Related Commands and Variables](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#related-commands-and-variables)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command#faq)

# !duel | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!duel` command allows users to challenge another user in chat to a duel, wagering their loyalty points. The challenged user then has a limited time to respond using [`!accept`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept)
 or [`!deny`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny)
.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To initiate a duel challenge, use the following syntax:

    !duel <username> <points>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

Challenger:!duel TargetUser 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@TargetUser, @Challenger wants to duel you for 100 points, you can !accept or !deny within 2 minutes

example chat

ViewerName:!duel SelfUser 50

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@SelfUser, you cannot duel yourself Kappa

example chat

ViewerName:!duel AnotherUser 10000

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, you do not have enough points to duel for 10000.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<username>` (Required): The exact username of the user you want to challenge.
*   `<points>` (Required): The number of loyalty points you want to wager. You must have at least this many points.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!duel` command requires the **Duel module** to be active. You can enable and configure it in your **StreamElements Dashboard** under `Chatbot` -> `Modules`.

Within the Duel module settings, you can customize:

*   **Maximum amount**: The highest number of points users can wager in a single duel.
*   **User cooldown**: How long (in seconds) an individual user must wait before initiating another duel after participating in one.
*   **Global cooldown**: How long (in seconds) everyone must wait after a duel finishes before _anyone_ can start a new one.
*   **Win message**: The chat message displayed when a user wins the duel.
    *   Available variables: `{winner}`, `{loser}`
*   **Points won message**: The chat message displayed when points are awarded after a duel.
    *   Available variables: `{winner}`, `{loser}`, `{points}`, `{pointsname}`

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!accept`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/accept)
    : Used by the challenged user to accept a duel.
*   [`!deny`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/deny)
    : Used by the challenged user to decline a duel.
*   [`!cancelduel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelduel)
    : Used by the challenger to cancel their _outgoing_ duel request.
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Check your current loyalty points balance.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel#related-commands)

---

# !emotes | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!emotes` command serves two primary functions:

1.  **List Platform Emotes:** When followed by a platform name (`twitch`, `bttv`, `ffz`, `7tv`), it lists the active emotes from that specific provider directly in chat.
2.  **Reload Emote Cache (Moderator+):** Using the `reload` keyword, moderators can refresh the bot's internal cache of emotes for **all** platforms (Twitch, BTTV, FFZ, 7TV) simultaneously.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**To list active emotes for a specific platform:**

    !emotes <platform>

*   `<platform>`: Required. The platform whose emotes you want to list. Valid options: `twitch`, `bttv`, `ffz`, `7tv`.

**To reload the emote cache:**

    !emotes reload

*   This refreshes the bot's internal cache of available emotes for **all** platforms (Twitch, BTTV, FFZ, 7TV).
*   It is useful if new emotes have been added or changed and aren't showing up correctly.

Permissions

Using `!emotes reload` requires **Moderator** permission level or higher by default. This can be adjusted in the StreamElements Dashboard under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Listing active FFZ emotes:**

example chat

ViewerName:!emotes ffz

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Active FrankerFaceZ emotes in chat: monkaS FeelsOkayMan PepeHands ZULUL

**Listing active BTTV emotes:**

example chat

ViewerName:!emotes bttv

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Active BetterTTV emotes in chat: Pog LULW monkaW Clap

**Reloading all emote caches (Moderator+):**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!emotes reload

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully updated emotes :)

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The `reload` function will refresh caches for Twitch and any enabled third-party integrations.
*   The bot needs appropriate permissions (usually just being present in chat) to fetch Twitch emotes.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!emotecount`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount)
    : Checks how many times a specific emote has been used in chat.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are no known aliases for the `!emotes` command.

# Chatbot Variables | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

New Variable

We've added a new AI variable! Check out the [$(ai) Variable](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/ai)
 documentation to learn how to integrate AI-generated responses into your chat commands.

Introduction to Variables in Chat Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables#introduction-to-variables-in-chat-commands "Direct link to Introduction to Variables in Chat Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Chat commands support variables in a dynamic way. Variables are placeholders that can be used in chat commands to represent a specific value or piece of information. When a command is triggered, these variables are replaced with the actual values they represent.

For example, in the command `${uptime shroud}`, `shroud` is a variable representing a username. When this command is executed, the `uptime` of the user `shroud` is returned.

Variables make chat commands more flexible and powerful, allowing for a wide range of interactions and functionalities.

In addition to the `${}` syntax, we also support the `$()` syntax for variables. Both of these syntaxes can be used interchangeably in chat commands. For instance, the command `${uptime shroud}` can also be written as `$(uptime shroud)`.

[📄️ $(7tvemotes)\
----------------\
\
Lists active 7TV emotes in a Twitch channel. Learn how to use the $(7tvemotes) variable in StreamElements Chatbot commands.](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/7tvemotes)

# !editcounter | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!editcounter` command allows streamers and moderators to modify the value of a pre-defined custom counter directly from chat. Counters are useful for tracking things like deaths in a game, wins, specific events, or any other metric you want to display or reference.

**Note:** Counters must first be created in the StreamElements Dashboard under `Chatbot` -> `Counters`.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To modify a counter, use the following syntax:

    !editcounter <counter_name> <value>

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!editcounter deaths +1

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, changed the deaths counter from 5 to 6.

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!editcounter wins 10

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Broadcaster, changed the wins counter from 9 to 10.

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!editcounter donations -5

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, changed the donations counter from 100 to 95.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<counter_name>` (Required): The exact name of the counter you created in the Dashboard (case-sensitive).
*   `<value>` (Required): The value to apply. It can be:
    *   A number (e.g., `15`): Sets the counter to this exact value.
    *   `+number` (e.g., `+1`): Increments the counter by this amount.
    *   `-number` (e.g., `-3`): Decrements the counter by this amount.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Counters must be created in the **StreamElements Dashboard** under `Chatbot` -> `Counters` before they can be edited via this command.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Variables[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#related-variables "Direct link to Related Variables")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `$(count <counter_name>)`: This variable displays the current value of the specified counter. It can be used in other commands or titles. Example: `!deathcount - Current deaths: $(count deaths)`

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#configuration)
    
*   [Related Variables](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/editcounter#related-variables)

# !emotecount | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!emotecount` command allows anyone in chat to check how many times a specific emote has been used in the channel's chat history (since tracking began).

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To check the count for a specific emote, use the following syntax:

    !emotecount <emote_name>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!emotecount Kappa

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, The emote Kappa has been used 15731 times! PogChamp

example chat

ViewerName:!emotecount channelCoolEmote

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, The emote channelCoolEmote has been used 452 times! PogChamp

example chat

ViewerName:!emotecount NonExistentEmote

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, The emote NonExistentEmote was not found. NotLikeThis

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<emote_name>` (Required): The exact name of the emote you want to check (case-sensitive). This can be a global emote, channel emote, or third-party emote (BTTV, FFZ, 7TV) if enabled.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Emote usage tracking is handled automatically by StreamElements when the bot is active in the channel.
*   The accuracy depends on when the bot joined and started tracking messages.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!emotes`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotes)
    : Provides a link to view the channel's available third-party emotes (BTTV, FFZ, 7TV).

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Why is the count different from what I expected?** The count reflects usage only since StreamElements started tracking messages in this channel. It might not include historical usage before the bot was added or if there were periods the bot was inactive.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#related-commands)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/emotecount#faq)
