# $(user) Variable | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `$(user)` variable in StreamElements Chatbot allows you to access and display various user-related information in your chat messages and commands. These variables provide data such as usernames, loyalty points, ranks, and activity timestamps.

Key Point

`$(user)` can accept an optional username argument to retrieve information about any user, not just the command sender. When used without arguments, it behaves similarly to [`$(sender)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/sender)
.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the `$(user)` variable, include it in your chat message or command response using the `$()` syntax. For example, `$(user)` will display the user's display name.

*   Without argument: `$(user)` refers to the command sender
*   With argument: `$(user username)` refers to the specified user

Available $(user) Variables[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#available-user-variables "Direct link to Available $(user) Variables")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### $(user)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#user "Direct link to $(user)")

Displays the user's display name.

**Example:**

    Current user: $(user)Current user: $(user adeithe)

**Output:**

    Current user: StylerCurrent user: Adeithe

### $(user.name)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#username "Direct link to $(user.name)")

Displays the user's display name in lowercase letters.

**Example:**

    Current user: $(user.name)Current user: $(user.name adeithe)

**Output:**

    Current user: stylerCurrent user: adeithe

### $(user.points)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userpoints "Direct link to $(user.points)")

Displays the user's loyalty currency owned.

**Example:**

    $(user) has $(user.points) points$(user adeithe) has $(user.points adeithe) points

**Output:**

    Styler has 100 pointsAdeithe has 150 points

### $(user.points\_rank)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userpoints_rank "Direct link to $(user.points_rank)")

Displays the user's rank on the loyalty currency leaderboard.

**Example:**

    $(user) is rank $(user.points_rank) on the leaderboard$(user adeithe) is rank $(user.points_rank adeithe) on the leaderboard

**Output:**

    Styler is rank 5/283 on the leaderboardAdeithe is rank 3/283 on the leaderboard

### $(user.points\_alltime\_rank)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userpoints_alltime_rank "Direct link to $(user.points_alltime_rank)")

Displays the user's rank on the all-time loyalty currency leaderboard.

**Example:**

    $(user) is rank $(user.points_alltime_rank) on the all-time leaderboard$(user adeithe) is rank $(user.points_alltime_rank adeithe) on the all-time leaderboard

**Output:**

    Styler is rank 5/283 on the all-time leaderboardAdeithe is rank 3/283 on the all-time leaderboard

### $(user.level)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlevel "Direct link to $(user.level)")

Displays the user's access level.

**Example:**

    $(user) is level $(user.level)$(user adeithe) is level $(user.level adeithe)

**Output:**

    Styler is level 2000Adeithe is level 2500

### $(user.lastmessage)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlastmessage "Direct link to $(user.lastmessage)")

Displays the user's last typed message in the chat.

**Example:**

    $(user) last typed: $(user.lastmessage)$(user adeithe) last typed: $(user.lastmessage adeithe)

**Output:**

    Styler last typed: !pointsAdeithe last typed: Hello everyone!

### $(user.lastseen)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlastseen "Direct link to $(user.lastseen)")

Displays the time that a user was most recently seen in the viewer list or chat.

**Example:**

    $(user) was last seen $(user.lastseen) ago$(user adeithe) was last seen $(user.lastseen adeithe) ago

**Output:**

    Styler was last seen 13m 15s agoAdeithe was last seen 5m 30s ago

### $(user.lastactive)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlastactive "Direct link to $(user.lastactive)")

Displays the time that a user most recently typed a message in the chat.

**Example:**

    $(user) was last active $(user.lastactive) ago$(user adeithe) was last active $(user.lastactive adeithe) ago

**Output:**

    Styler was last active 13m 15s agoAdeithe was last active 5m 30s ago

### $(user.time\_online)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usertime_online "Direct link to $(user.time_online)")

Displays the total time a user has spent watching the stream.

**Example:**

    $(user) has been watching the stream for $(user.time_online)$(user adeithe) has been watching the stream for $(user.time_online adeithe)

**Output:**

    Styler has been watching the stream for 27m 16sAdeithe has been watching the stream for 1h 15m 45s

### $(user.time\_online\_rank)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usertime_online_rank "Direct link to $(user.time_online_rank)")

Displays the user's rank on the leaderboard for online time watched.

**Example:**

    $(user) is rank $(user.time_online_rank) on the online leaderboard$(user adeithe) is rank $(user.time_online_rank adeithe) on the online leaderboard

**Output:**

    Styler is rank 5/283 on the online leaderboardAdeithe is rank 2/283 on the online leaderboard

### $(user.time\_offline\_rank)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usertime_offline_rank "Direct link to $(user.time_offline_rank)")

Displays the user's rank on the leaderboard for offline time watched.

**Example:**

    $(user) is rank $(user.time_offline_rank) on the offline leaderboard$(user adeithe) is rank $(user.time_offline_rank adeithe) on the offline leaderboard

**Output:**

    Styler is rank 5/283 on the offline leaderboardAdeithe is rank 2/283 on the offline leaderboard

Best Practices[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Use `$(user)` without arguments when you need information about the command trigger.
2.  Use `$(user username)` when you need to reference other users or allow flexible user queries.
3.  Always provide clear examples and explanations when creating custom commands using these variables.

Troubleshooting[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#troubleshooting "Direct link to Troubleshooting")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   If a variable returns unexpected results, ensure you're using the correct syntax and that the user exists in your channel's database.
*   Remember that `$(user)` variables can accept arguments. If you only need information about the command sender, consider using [`$(sender)`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/sender)
     instead.

Related Documentation[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#related-documentation "Direct link to Related Documentation")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   For information specifically about the command sender, see the [`$(sender)` variable documentation](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/sender)
    .
*   For more detailed information on StreamElements variables and commands, refer to the official [StreamElements Documentation](https://dev.streamelements.com/docs)
    .

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usage)
    
*   [Available $(user) Variables](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#available-user-variables)
    *   [$(user)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#user)
        
    *   [$(user.name)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#username)
        
    *   [$(user.points)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userpoints)
        
    *   [$(user.points\_rank)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userpoints_rank)
        
    *   [$(user.points\_alltime\_rank)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userpoints_alltime_rank)
        
    *   [$(user.level)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlevel)
        
    *   [$(user.lastmessage)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlastmessage)
        
    *   [$(user.lastseen)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlastseen)
        
    *   [$(user.lastactive)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#userlastactive)
        
    *   [$(user.time\_online)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usertime_online)
        
    *   [$(user.time\_online\_rank)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usertime_online_rank)
        
    *   [$(user.time\_offline\_rank)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#usertime_offline_rank)
        
*   [Best Practices](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#best-practices)
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#troubleshooting)
    
*   [Related Documentation](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/variables/user#related-documentation)

# !permit | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!permit` command temporarily exempts a specified user from the bot's automatic link filtering/timeout system. This allows them to post links for a short duration without being punished.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To grant temporary link permission:

    !permit <username> [duration_seconds]

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Permit a user for the default 60 seconds:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!permit HelpfulViewer

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@HelpfulViewer, you have been permitted to post links for 60 seconds.

**Permit a user for 120 seconds:**

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!permit TrustedFriend 120

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@TrustedFriend, you have been permitted to post links for 120 seconds.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<username>` (Required): The exact username of the viewer to permit.
*   `[duration_seconds]` (Optional): The duration (in seconds) the permit should last. Defaults to 60 seconds if not specified.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command relies on the **Link Protection** filter being enabled within the `Chatbot` -> `Spam Filters` section of the StreamElements Dashboard.
*   The default permit duration (if not specified in the command) can be configured in the Link Protection filter settings.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!level`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/level)
    : Used to view or set a user's permanent permission level, which can also control link permissions.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/permit#related-commands)

# !play | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!play` command (aliased as `!resume` and `!unpause`) resumes the playback of the StreamElements media request queue after it has been stopped by the [`!pause`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/pause)
 command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To resume playback:

    !play

Or using aliases:

    !resume!unpause

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!play

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, Media request playback resumed!

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!pause`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/pause)
    : Pauses the current media playback.
*   [`!skip`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip)
    : Skips the currently playing media item.
*   [`!volume`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/volume)
    : Adjusts the volume of the media player.
*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Adds a song/video to the queue.
*   [`!songqueue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue)
    : Provides a link to the media queue page.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `!resume`
*   `!unpause`

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#examples)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#related-commands)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play#aliases)

# !points | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!points` command allows anyone in chat to check the loyalty point balance and leaderboard rank of themselves or another specified user.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To check points and rank:

    !points [username]

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Checking your own points:**

example chat

Viewer1:!points

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Viewer1, you have 5280 ChannelPoints and are rank #15 on the leaderboard.

**Checking another user's points:**

example chat

ViewerName:!points StreamElements

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@StreamElements has 99999 ChannelPoints and is rank #1 on the leaderboard.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `[username]` (Optional): The exact username of the user whose points you want to check. If omitted, it defaults to the user running the command.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command requires the **Loyalty system** to be active. Enable and configure it in your **StreamElements Dashboard** under `Loyalty` -> `Loyalty Settings`.
*   The name of the loyalty points currency (e.g., "ChannelPoints" in the example) is customizable in the Loyalty Settings.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!top`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top)
    : Shows the top users on the leaderboard directly in chat.
*   [`!leaderboard`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/leaderboard)
    : Provides a link to the full leaderboard page.
*   [`!givepoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/givepoints)
    : Allows users to transfer points to each other.
*   [`!addpoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints)
     / [`!setpoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints)
    : (Moderator+) Commands to modify user points.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points#related-commands)

# !quote | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!quote` command interacts with the channel's quote system. Viewers can use it to display a random saved quote. Moderators and the broadcaster can use subcommands to add new quotes or remove existing ones.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**To display a random quote:**

    !quote

**To display a specific quote by ID:**

    !quote <quote_id>

**To add a quote (Moderator+):**

    !quote add <quote_text>

**To remove a quote (Moderator+):**

    !quote remove <quote_id>

**Important:** Adding (`add`) and removing (`remove`) quotes typically requires **Moderator** permission level or higher.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Displaying a random quote:**

example chat

ViewerName:!quote

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Quote #42: "This is peak gameplay!" - Added by Moderator1 (Jan 15, 2024)

**Displaying a specific quote:**

example chat

ViewerName:!quote 10

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Quote #10: "I can't believe that worked!" - Added by Broadcaster (Dec 25, 2023)

**Adding a new quote (Moderator+):**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!quote add Never give up!

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully added quote #51.

**Removing a quote (Moderator+):**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!quote remove 51

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, successfully removed quote #51.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<quote_id>` (Optional): The specific ID number of the quote to display or remove.
*   `add <quote_text>` (Moderator+): The subcommand `add` followed by the text of the quote to save.
*   `remove <quote_id>` (Moderator+): The subcommand `remove` followed by the ID of the quote to delete.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The permission levels for adding and removing quotes can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Variables[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#related-variables "Direct link to Related Variables")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `$(quote <id>)`: Variable to display a specific quote by ID.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `!quote add`: `!quote +`
*   `!quote remove`: `!quote -`

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#configuration)
    
*   [Related Variables](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#related-variables)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/quote#aliases)

---

# !queue | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!queue` command suite helps manage a viewer queue, often used for activities like playing games with the streamer. It allows viewers to join, check their position, and moderators to manage the queue (open, close, pick, remove).

**Important:** Most subcommands (`open`, `close`, `pause`, `unpause`, `pick`, `remove`) typically require **Moderator** permission level or higher.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The general syntax follows this pattern:

    !queue <subcommand> [arguments...]

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here's a breakdown of common subcommands:

### `join`[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#join "Direct link to join")

Allows a viewer to enter the open queue.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue join`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ViewerName:!queue join
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, you have been added to the queue in position #5.
    

### `leave`[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#leave "Direct link to leave")

Allows a viewer to remove themselves from the queue.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue leave`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ViewerName:!queue leave
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, you have been removed from the queue.
    

### `position`[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#position "Direct link to position")

Checks the command user's current position in the queue.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue position`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ViewerName:!queue position
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, you are currently position #3 in the queue.
    

### `list`[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#list "Direct link to list")

Provides a link to view the full queue.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue list`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ViewerName:!queue list
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:View the queue here: https://streamelements.com/YOUR\_CHANNEL/queue
    

### `open` (Moderator+)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#open-moderator "Direct link to open-moderator")

Opens the queue, allowing viewers to join.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue open`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!queue open
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, The queue is now open! Viewers can type !queue join to enter.
    

### `close` (Moderator+)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#close-moderator "Direct link to close-moderator")

Closes the queue, preventing new viewers from joining.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue close`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!queue close
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, The queue is now closed.
    

### `pause` (Moderator+)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#pause-moderator "Direct link to pause-moderator")

Temporarily stops viewers from joining the queue (similar to close, but implies temporary).

*   **Syntax:** `!queue pause`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!queue pause
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, The queue is paused.
    

### `unpause` (Moderator+)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#unpause-moderator "Direct link to unpause-moderator")

Resumes allowing viewers to join the paused queue.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue unpause`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!queue unpause
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, The queue is no longer paused.
    

### `pick [random | <username>]` (Moderator+)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#pick-random--username-moderator "Direct link to pick-random--username-moderator")

Selects the next participant from the queue.

*   **Syntax:**
    *   `!queue pick random` (Selects randomly)
    *   `!queue pick <username>` (Selects a specific user)
    *   `!queue pick` (Often defaults to picking the user at position #1)
*   **Example (random):**
    
    example chat
    
    ![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!queue pick random
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@LuckyViewer has been randomly selected from the queue!
    
*   **Example (specific):**
    
    example chat
    
    ![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!queue pick SpecificUser
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@SpecificUser has been picked from the queue!
    

### `remove <username>` (Moderator+)[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#remove-username-moderator "Direct link to remove-username-moderator")

Removes a specific user from the queue.

*   **Syntax:** `!queue remove <username>`
*   **Example:**
    
    example chat
    
    ![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!queue remove ProblemUser
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, ProblemUser has been removed from the queue.
    

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The **Queue module** must be enabled in your StreamElements Dashboard under `Chatbot` -> `Modules`.
*   Queue settings (like max size, subscriber luck, messages) are configured within the module settings on the Dashboard.
*   Permission levels for subcommands can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command is self-contained for queue management.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#examples)
    *   [`join`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#join)
        
    *   [`leave`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#leave)
        
    *   [`position`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#position)
        
    *   [`list`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#list)
        
    *   [`open` (Moderator+)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#open-moderator)
        
    *   [`close` (Moderator+)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#close-moderator)
        
    *   [`pause` (Moderator+)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#pause-moderator)
        
    *   [`unpause` (Moderator+)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#unpause-moderator)
        
    *   [`pick [random | <username>]` (Moderator+)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#pick-random--username-moderator)
        
    *   [`remove <username>` (Moderator+)](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#remove-username-moderator)
        
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/queue#related-commands)

# !redeem | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!redeem` command allows viewers to exchange their loyalty points for items listed in the channel's StreamElements **Stream Store**.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To redeem an item:

    !redeem <item_name>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Redeeming a sound effect named "Air Horn":**

example chat

ViewerName:!redeem Air Horn

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User successfully redeemed Air Horn for 100 points!

**Trying to redeem an item the user can't afford:**

example chat

ViewerName:!redeem Expensive Item

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, you do not have enough points to redeem Expensive Item (Cost: 5000).

**Trying to redeem a disabled or non-existent item:**

example chat

ViewerName:!redeem Old Item

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, item "Old Item" not found or is not available.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<item_name>` (Required): The exact name of the store item to redeem (case-sensitive). Find item names on the store page (link via `!items` command).

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Stream Store** and **Loyalty System** to be active and configured (`Chatbot` -> `Modules` and `Loyalty` -> `Loyalty Settings` / `Stream Store`).
*   Items must be created in the Stream Store with names, costs, cooldowns, etc.
*   Items must be enabled to be redeemable.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!items`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/items)
    : Provides a link to the store page listing available items.
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Checks the user's current point balance.
*   [`!closestore`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/closestore)
     / [`!openstore`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/openstore)
    : (Moderator+) Enable/disable regular store items.
*   [`!disablesfx`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/disablesfx)
     / [`!enablesfx`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/enablesfx)
    : (Moderator+) Enable/disable SFX store items.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/redeem#related-commands)

---

# !setpoints | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!setpoints` command allows streamers and moderators to set a specific number of loyalty points for a user in the chat. This command is useful for managing loyalty programs, rewarding viewers, or correcting point balances.

caution

Using this command will **overwrite** the user's current point balance. Use [`!addpoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints)
 if you want to add to their balance instead.

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set a user's point balance:

    !setpoints <username> <points>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!setpoints darkoe 1000

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, set darkoe's points to 1000!

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!setpoints viewer123 0

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Broadcaster, set viewer123's points to 0!

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<username>` (Required): The username of the viewer whose points you want to set.
*   `<points>` (Required): The new amount of points to assign to the user.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command requires the **Loyalty system** to be active (`Loyalty` -> `Loyalty Settings`).
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!addpoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/addpoints)
    : Adds points to a user's balance without overwriting.
*   [`!givepoints`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/givepoints)
    : Allows users to transfer points.
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Checks a user's current point balance.
*   [`!top`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top)
    : View the leaderboard for points.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setpoints#examples)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!setgame` command allows streamers and moderators to update the current game category of a Twitch stream in real-time. This feature ensures that viewers always have accurate information about the content being streamed.

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setgame#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator changed the game to "Fortnite"!

*   `<game>` (Required): The title of the game you want to set for your stream. This parameter supports fuzzy searching, allowing for slight misspellings or common abbreviations.

    : Displays how long the stream has been live.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/setgame#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

# !removesong | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!removesong` command allows streamers and moderators to remove entries from the StreamElements media request queue. It can target either a specific song via its URL or all songs requested by a particular user.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To remove a specific song by its URL:

    !removesong <song_url>

To remove all songs requested by a specific user:

    !removesong <username>

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Removing a specific song by URL:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!removesong https://youtu.be/dQw4w9WgXcQ

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, Rick Astley - Never Gonna Give You Up was removed from the queue.

**Removing all songs requested by a user:**

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!removesong SpamRequester

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Broadcaster, All songs requested by SpamRequester have been removed.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<song_url>` OR `<username>` (Required): You must provide _either_ the direct URL of the song/video to remove _or_ the exact username of the person whose requests should be removed.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Adds a song/video to the queue.
*   [`!songqueue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue)
    : Provides a link to the media queue page.
*   [`!skip`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip)
    : Skips the _currently playing_ song.
*   [`!play`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play)
     / [`!pause`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/pause)
    : Controls playback.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong#usage)

# !roulette | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#overview "Direct link to Overview")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!roulette` command allows viewers to gamble a specified amount of their loyalty points. They have a chance to double their bet or lose it all.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#usage "Direct link to Usage")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To play roulette:

    !roulette <amount_or_%>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#examples "Direct link to Examples")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Betting 100 points:**

example chat

ViewerName:!roulette 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User spins the wheel... and wins 100 points! You now have 1100 points. PogChamp

**Betting 50% of points:**

example chat

ViewerName:!roulette 50%

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User spins the wheel... and lost 500 points! You now have 500 points. FeelsBadMan

**Betting all points:**

example chat

ViewerName:!roulette all

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User spins the wheel... and lost 1000 points! You now have 0 points. FeelsBadMan

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<amount_or_%>` (Required): The number of points to bet. This can be:
    *   A specific number (e.g., `100`).
    *   A percentage of the user's current points (e.g., `50%`).
    *   A number with `k` for thousands (e.g., `5k`).
    *   A number with `m` for millions (e.g., `1m`).
    *   The keyword `all` to bet all points.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Roulette module** and **Loyalty system** to be active.
*   Configure settings in the **Roulette module** on the Dashboard (`Chatbot` -> `Modules`). Available options include:
    *   **Enable/Disable Module:** Toggle the roulette game on or off.
    *   **Rig Percentage:** Adjust the win chance using a slider (0% = Never lose, 100% = Always lose).
    *   **Minimum Amount:** Set the minimum number of points required to play (Default: 1).
    *   **User Cooldown:** Set the minimum time (in seconds) a specific user must wait before playing again (Default: 60).
    *   **Global Cooldown:** Set the minimum time (in seconds) everyone must wait after a roulette spin before anyone can play again (Default: 0).
    *   **Win Message:** Customize the message shown when a user wins.
        *   _Available variables:_ `{user}`, `{bet}`, `{points}`, `{pointsname}`
        *   _Default:_ `/me {user} won {bet} ${pointsname} in roulette and now has {points} ${pointsname}! FeelsGoodMan`
    *   **Lose Message:** Customize the message shown when a user loses.
        *   _Available variables:_ `{user}`, `{bet}`, `{points}`, `{pointsname}`
        *   _Default:_ `/me {user} lost {bet} ${pointsname} in roulette and now has {points} ${pointsname}! FeelsBadMan`
    *   **All-in Win Message:** Customize the message shown when a user bets `all` and wins.
        *   _Available variables:_ `{user}`, `{bet}`, `{points}`, `{pointsname}`
        *   _Default:_ `/me PogChamp {user} went all in and won {bet} ${pointsname} PogChamp they now have {points} ${pointsname} FeelsGoodMan`
    *   **All-in Lose Message:** Customize the message shown when a user bets `all` and loses.
        *   _Available variables:_ `{user}`, `{bet}`, `{points}`, `{pointsname}`
        *   _Default:_ `/me {user} went all in and lost every single one of their {bet} ${pointsname} LUL`

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Check current point balance.
*   [`!duel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel)
     / [`!slots`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots)
     / [`!bet`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet)
    : Other points-based games (if enabled).

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette#related-commands)

---

# !slots | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!slots` command allows viewers to play a simple slot machine game in your chat. Users bet a certain amount of loyalty points and have a chance to win a multiple of their bet back based on matching emotes.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To play the slot machine:

    !slots <bet>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!slots 100

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User you got Kappa | Kappa | Keepo and lost your 100 points LUL

example chat

ViewerName:!slots 500

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User you got Kappa | Kappa | Kappa and won 1500 points PogChamp

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<bet>` (Required): The amount of loyalty points the user wants to bet. This must be a positive integer and within the configured minimum/maximum bet limits.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Streamers can customize the `!slots` game through the **Slots module** settings on the StreamElements dashboard (`Chatbot` -> `Modules`):

*   **Module Toggle:** Enable or disable the entire `!slots` game.
*   **System Rigging:** Adjust the payout percentage. A value lower than 100% means viewers are statistically likely to lose points over time, while a value higher than 100% means they are likely to gain points. The default is often set to ensure a house edge. _(Example: 200% in the provided image)_
*   **Minimum Points:** Set the minimum number of loyalty points a viewer must have to play the slot machine. _(Example: 100 points in the image)_
*   **Emotes:** Choose which emotes will act as the symbols on the slot machine reels. _(Examples from image: Kappa, PogChamp, BibleThump, OpieOP, 4Head)_
*   **Cooldowns:**
    *   **User Cooldown:** The minimum time (in seconds) a specific user must wait before playing again. _(Example: 60 seconds in the image)_
    *   **Global Cooldown:** The minimum time (in seconds) before _anyone_ can use the `!slots` command again after it's been used. _(Example: 0 seconds in the image)_
*   **Win Message:** Customize the message displayed when a viewer wins. Available arguments: `{user}`, `{points}`, `{emotes}`, `{pointsname}`. _(Example from image: `@​{user} you got {emotes} and won {points} ${pointsname} PogChamp //`)_
*   **Lose Message:** Customize the message displayed when a viewer loses. Available arguments: `{user}`, `{points}`, `{emotes}`, `{pointsname}`. _(Example from image: `@​{user} you got {emotes} and lost your {points} ${pointsname} LUL`)_

important

The **Loyalty system** must also be active for the `!slots` command to function, as it relies on loyalty points.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Check your current loyalty points balance.
*   [`!roulette`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/roulette)
     / [`!duel`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/duel)
     / [`!bet`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/bet)
    : Other points-based games (if enabled).

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/slots#related-commands)

---

# !skip | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!skip` command is used to skip the currently playing song in the StreamElements media request queue. This command is useful for streamers and moderators who want to quickly move to the next song in the queue.

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the `!skip` command, simply type it in the chat:

    !skip

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!skip

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, skipped song: Drake, 21 Savage - Rich Flex (Audio)

example chat

ViewerName:!skip

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, you do not have permission to use that command.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!song`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song)
    : Displays information about the currently playing song.
*   [`!next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/next)
    : Displays information about the next song in the queue.
*   [`!songqueue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue)
    : Shows the current media request queue.
*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Adds a song to the media request queue.
*   [`!removesong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong)
    : Removes a song from the queue.
*   [`!play`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play)
     / [`!pause`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/pause)
    : Controls playback.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

*   `!ns`

# !song | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!song` command allows viewers to retrieve information about the currently playing song in the StreamElements media request queue. This command is useful for viewers who want to know the title, artist, and requester of the current song.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the `!song` command, simply type it in the chat:

    !song

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!song

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, current song: DrakeVEVO - Drake, 21 Savage - Rich Flex (Audio), requested by styler https://youtu.be/I4DjHHVHWAE

example chat

ViewerName:!song

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, No song is currently playing.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command requires the **Media Request** module to be enabled and configured in your StreamElements Dashboard (`Chatbot` -> `Modules`).
*   The information displayed depends on the media source (e.g., YouTube, Spotify) and the data available for the requested track.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Used to add songs to the media request queue.
*   [`!skip`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip)
    : (Moderator+) Used to skip the current song.
*   [`!next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/next)
    : Shows details about the _next_ song in the queue.
*   [`!songqueue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue)
    : Shows the upcoming songs in the media request queue.
*   [`!play`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play)
     / [`!pause`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/pause)
    : (Moderator+) Controls playback.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song#overview)
