# !ticket | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#overview "Direct link to Overview")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!ticket` command allows viewers to purchase tickets for ongoing giveaways using their loyalty points. This command enables participation in raffles hosted through the StreamElements loyalty system.

Important Note

By default, the `!ticket` command does **not** reply to the user to prevent chat spam during active giveaways. Streamers can enable confirmation messages by checking the "Send confirmation when buying tickets in chat" option in the giveaway settings on the StreamElements dashboard.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To purchase tickets, type `!ticket` in the chat, optionally followed by the number of tickets you wish to buy. If no number is specified, it defaults to purchasing one ticket.

**Syntax:**

    !ticket [*number_of_tickets*]

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Buying a single ticket:**
    
    example chat
    
    ViewerName:!ticket
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@viewer, you successfully bought 1 ticket!
    
2.  **Buying multiple tickets:**
    
    example chat
    
    ViewerName:!ticket 5
    
    ![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@viewer, you successfully bought 5 tickets!
    
    _(Note: The reply is only sent if enabled by the streamer)_
    

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `number_of_tickets` | Optional | The number of tickets to purchase. Defaults to `1` if omitted. Must be a positive whole number. |

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!giveaway`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/giveaway)
    : Used by moderators to start or manage giveaways.
*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Allows users to check their current loyalty points balance.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `!enter`

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Streamers configure giveaway settings, including ticket cost and the maximum number of tickets a viewer can purchase per giveaway, through the StreamElements dashboard under **Loyalty -> Contests & Giveaways**.

FAQ[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#faq "Direct link to FAQ")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **What happens if I try to buy more tickets than I have points for?** The command will fail, and you won't purchase any tickets. You might receive an error message depending on the bot's configuration, or the command might silently fail.
*   **Can I buy tickets if there's no giveaway running?** No, the `!ticket` command only works when a giveaway is active.
*   **Is there a maximum number of tickets I can buy?** Yes, the streamer sets a maximum number of tickets per user for each giveaway in the StreamElements dashboard.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#parameters)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#related-commands)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#aliases)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#configuration)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/ticket#faq)

---

# !sraffle | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!sraffle` command allows streamers and moderators to start a **raffle**, typically allowing only a **single entry per viewer**. The command will randomly select **one winner** from all the viewers who entered using the [`!join`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/join)
 command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start a single-entry raffle:

    !sraffle [win_points] [duration_seconds]

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Start a raffle awarding 10 points, lasting 10 seconds:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!sraffle 10 10

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:a Raffle has begun for 10 points PogChamp it will end in 10 Seconds. Enter by typing "!join" OpieOP

**Start a raffle using default settings (100 points, 30 seconds):**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!sraffle

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:a Raffle has begun for 100 points PogChamp it will end in 30 Seconds. Enter by typing "!join" OpieOP

**Start a raffle awarding 0 points, lasting 60 seconds:**

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!sraffle 0 60

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:A raffle has started! Enter by typing "!join". Ends in 60 seconds.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `[win_points]` (Optional): The amount of loyalty points awarded to the winner. Defaults to `100` if not specified. Requires the Loyalty module to be active.
*   `[duration_seconds]` (Optional): How long the raffle entry period lasts (in **seconds**). Defaults to `30` seconds if not specified.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Raffle module** to be active (`Chatbot` -> `Modules`).
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.
*   Other settings like the default duration (in seconds) and raffle messages can be configured in the Raffle module settings on the Dashboard. The entry command is typically fixed to `!join` for `!sraffle`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!join`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/join)
    : The command viewers use to enter an active `!sraffle`.
*   [`!raffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/raffle)
    : (Moderator+) Starts a points-based, multi-entry raffle where points are spent to enter.
*   [`!cancelraffle`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/cancelraffle)
    : (Moderator+) Cancels the currently active raffle (`!raffle` or `!sraffle`).
*   [`!giveaway`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/giveaway)
    : Checks the status of the main channel giveaway.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/sraffle#related-commands)

---

# !songrequest | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!songrequest` command (aliased as `!sr`) allows viewers to add songs or videos to the streamer's media request queue. This command primarily integrates with YouTube, enabling users to request media using search terms or direct URLs.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To request media:

    !songrequest <search_term_or_url>

Or using the alias:

    !sr <search_term_or_url>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!songrequest epic sax guy

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, added "Epic Sax Guy 10 Hours" to the queue at #2 (playing ~in 3 mins 5 secs) https://youtu.be/kxopViU98Xo

example chat

ViewerName:!sr https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dQw4w9WgXcQ

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, added "Rick Astley - Never Gonna Give You Up" to the queue at #3 (playing ~in 7 mins 15 secs) https://youtu.be/dQw4w9WgXcQ

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<search_term_or_url>` (Required): The media to request. This can be:
    *   A YouTube video URL.
    *   A YouTube playlist URL (if enabled in settings).
    *   A search term (the bot will typically pick the first result).

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Media Request** module to be enabled and configured (`Chatbot` -> `Modules`).
*   Streamers can configure various settings in the Media Request module:
    *   Enable/disable the feature.
    *   Link a Spotify account (optional, for different functionality).
    *   Set request limits (per user, per stream).
    *   Define user level restrictions for requesting.
    *   Set maximum song/video duration.
    *   Enable/disable playlist requests.
    *   Set up a song blacklist (by keyword or specific URL).
    *   Configure point costs or subscriber-only access.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!songqueue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue)
    : View the current media request queue.
*   [`!song`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song)
    : Displays information about the currently playing song.
*   [`!next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/next)
    : Displays information about the next song in the queue.
*   [`!wrongsong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong)
    : Allows users to remove their most recent song request.
*   [`!skip`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip)
    : (Moderator+) Skips the currently playing song.
*   [`!volume`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/volume)
    : (Moderator+) Adjusts the volume of the media player.
*   [`!removesong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong)
    : (Moderator+) Removes a specific song or all songs by a user.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `!sr`

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#related-commands)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest#aliases)

# !srclear | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!srclear` command is used to clear the **entire** media request queue in your StreamElements chatbot. This command is particularly useful for streamers and moderators who want to reset the list of requested songs or videos during a stream.

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#usage "Direct link to Usage")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To clear the queue, simply type the command in chat:

    !srclear

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!srclear

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, Songrequest queue has been cleared!

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Used to request a song.
*   [`!removesong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/removesong)
    : Removes a specific song or all songs by a user.
*   [`!wrongsong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong)
    : Allows users to remove their most recent song request.
*   [`!skip`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip)
    : Skips the currently playing song in the queue.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `!clearsr`
*   `!clearsongs`
*   `!resetqueue`

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#examples)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#related-commands)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/srclear#aliases)

# !songqueue | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!songqueue` command provides viewers with a direct link to the channel's public StreamElements media request queue page. This allows them to see upcoming songs or videos without needing access to the streamer's dashboard.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type `!songqueue` in the chat to receive a link to the media request queue page:

    !songqueue

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!songqueue

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:You can see the current song request queue here: https://streamelements.com/YOUR\_CHANNEL/mediarequest

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The linked page shows requests that are currently in the queue.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
     / `!sr`: Used to request a song or media to be added to the queue.
*   [`!wrongsong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong)
    : Allows users to remove their most recent song request from the queue.
*   [`!song`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song)
    : Displays information about the currently playing song or media.
*   [`!next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/next)
    : Displays information about the next song in the queue.

*   `!requests`

# !vanish | StreamElements Docs

Twitch

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!vanish` command allows chatters to temporarily time themselves out for 1 second. On platforms like Twitch, this has the effect of clearing their recent messages from the chat window for other users.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/vanish#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the `!vanish` command, simply type it in the chat:

    !vanish

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/vanish#examples "Direct link to Examples")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!vanish

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:StreamElements timed out \[User\] for 1 second.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/vanish#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command is typically enabled by default.
*   Its functionality relies on the bot having timeout permissions (usually inherent).
*   The command can be enabled/disabled or have its permissions changed in the `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands` section of the StreamElements dashboard.

# !top | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!top` command displays the top users in chat based on either loyalty points or watch time, depending on the parameter provided. It provides a quick glimpse of the leaderboard directly within the chat interface.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To view a specific leaderboard:

    !top <type>

If `<type>` is omitted, the bot typically lists the available leaderboard types.

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!top points

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Top 5 ChannelPoints: 1. UserA (15000), 2. UserB (12500), 3. UserC (11000), 4. UserD (9800), 5. UserE (9500)

example chat

ViewerName:!top online

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Top 5 Online Watchtime: 1. UserC (50h 10m), 2. UserA (45h 30m), 3. UserE (42h 5m), 4. UserB (40h 15m), 5. UserF (38h 0m)

example chat

ViewerName:!top

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Available Commands: !top points/alltime/online/offline. You can see the ChannelPoints Leaderboard here: https://streamelements.com/StreamerName/leaderboard

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<type>` (Optional): The type of leaderboard to display. Common valid options are:
    
    *   `points`: Shows the top users based on loyalty points.
    *   `time` / `watchtime` / `alltime`: Displays the leaderboard based on total watch time (exact keyword may vary).
    *   `online`: Shows the top users based on watch time while the stream was live.
    *   `offline`: Displays the top users based on watch time while the stream was offline (if tracked).
    
    _(Check the output of `!top` without parameters or your Loyalty settings for the exact available types.)_
    

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Loyalty system** to be active (`Loyalty` -> `Loyalty Settings`).
*   The leaderboards displayed depend on the Loyalty module configuration (points tracking, watch time tracking enabled).
*   The name of the points currency (e.g., "ChannelPoints") is set in Loyalty Settings.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Checks an individual user's points and rank.
*   [`!watchtime`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime)
    : Checks an individual user's watch time.
*   [`!leaderboard`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/leaderboard)
    : Provides a link to the full web-based leaderboard.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top#related-commands)

The `!tip` command provides a convenient way for viewers to access the streamer's tipping link directly in chat. When used, it generates a message containing a URL where viewers can make monetary contributions to support the streamer via StreamElements.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/tip#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To display the tipping link, simply type the command in chat:

    !tip

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:You can Tip to StreamerName using this link https://streamelements.com/StreamerName/tip

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/tip#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The command is usually enabled by default.

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!volume` command allows moderators to check or adjust the volume level of the StreamElements media request player.

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/volume#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**To check the current volume:**

    !volume

**To set a new volume level:**

    !volume <level>

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!volume

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/volume#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<level>` (Optional): A number between `0` and `100` representing the desired volume percentage. If omitted, the command displays the current volume.

    : Skips the currently playing media request.
*   [`!play`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/play)
     / [`!pause`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/pause)
    : Controls media playback.

# !timer | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#overview "Direct link to Overview")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!timer` command allows moderators to enable or disable specific chat timers directly from the chat interface. Timers are messages automatically posted by the bot at set intervals.

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#usage "Direct link to Usage")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To enable or disable a timer:

    !timer <enable | disable> <timer_id_or_name>

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#examples "Direct link to Examples")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!timer enable socialMediaTimer

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Moderator, timer socialMediaTimer has been enabled.

example chat

![broadcaster badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/5527c58c-fb7d-422d-b71b-f309dcb85cc1/3 "broadcaster")BroadcasterName:!timer disable upcomingEvent

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@Broadcaster, timer upcomingEvent has been disabled.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<enable | disable>` (Required): The action to perform. `enable` turns the timer on, `disable` turns it off.
*   `<timer_id_or_name>` (Required): The ID or exact Name of the timer as configured in the StreamElements Dashboard.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Timers must be created and configured in the **StreamElements Dashboard** under `Chatbot` -> `Timers`.
*   You can find the Timer ID or set a specific Name in the timer's settings on the Dashboard.
*   The command's permission level can be adjusted under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!command`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/command)
    : Manages custom commands, which can sometimes serve similar purposes to simple timers.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/timer#related-commands)

# !votekick | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#overview "Direct link to Overview")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!votekick` command initiates a community vote to temporarily remove (timeout) a user from the chat. This allows viewers to participate in moderation by collectively deciding if a user should be kicked for a period.

**Important:** By default, only users with **Moderator** permission level or higher can use this command to _start_ a vote.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#usage "Direct link to Usage")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start a vote to kick a user:

    !votekick <username> [duration]

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#examples "Direct link to Examples")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Start a votekick for "DisruptiveUser" with the default vote duration:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!votekick DisruptiveUser

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Vote started to kick DisruptiveUser! Type !yes or !no to vote. (Vote ends in 60s)

**Start a votekick for "RuleBreaker" with a 2-minute vote duration:**

example chat

![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")ModUser:!votekick RuleBreaker 2m

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:Vote started to kick RuleBreaker! Type !yes or !no to vote. (Vote ends in 120s)

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `<username>` (Required): The exact username of the user to potentially kick.
*   `[duration]` (Optional): The length of time the _voting period_ should last.
    *   If not specified, uses the default duration set in the module configuration.
    *   Can be specified in seconds (`s`), minutes (`m`), or hours (`h`) (e.g., `90s`, `3m`).
    *   Note: This is the duration for voting, _not_ the kick/timeout duration if the vote passes.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Votekick module** to be enabled (`Chatbot` -> `Modules`).
*   Moderators configure settings in the **Votekick module** on the Dashboard:
    *   Enable/disable the module.
    *   Set the default **Vote Duration**.
    *   Set the required **Minimum Votes** for the vote to be considered valid.
    *   Define the **Vote Threshold** (percentage of `!yes` votes needed to pass).
    *   Set the **Timeout Duration** (how long the user is kicked if the vote passes).
    *   Establish **Cooldowns** (global and per-user for starting votes).

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/votekick#configuration)

---

# !voteskip | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch YouTube Trovo Kick

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#overview "Direct link to Overview")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!voteskip` command allows viewers to vote towards skipping the currently playing song or video in the StreamElements media request queue. If enough votes are cast (based on streamer configuration), the current item is skipped.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#usage "Direct link to Usage")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To cast a vote to skip the current media:

    !voteskip

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#examples "Direct link to Examples")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!voteskip

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User Skip requested! Current song will be skipped in 4 more votes!

example chat

ViewerName:!voteskip

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User Vote to skip successful! Skipping to the next media request.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Media Request** module to be enabled.
*   The **Vote Skip** feature must be enabled within the Media Request module settings on the StreamElements Dashboard.
*   Streamers configure the **Number of votes required to skip** in the module settings.
*   Other related settings might include cooldowns or user level restrictions for voting.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!song`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song)
    : Displays information about the currently playing song or media.
*   [`!next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/next)
    : Displays information about the next song in the queue.
*   [`!wrongsong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong)
    : Allows users to remove their own song request from the queue.
*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Lets viewers request songs or media to be played.
*   [`!skip`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/skip)
    : (Moderator+) Immediately skips the current media.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#examples)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/voteskip#related-commands)

# !watchtime | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!watchtime` command allows viewers to check how long they've accumulated watching the current channel. This feature requires the Loyalty system to be active and configured to track watch time.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To check watch time:

    !watchtime [username]

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!watchtime

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User has spent 2 hours and 15 minutes watching StreamerName!

example chat

ViewerName:!watchtime LoyalViewer

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:LoyalViewer has spent 1 day 5 hours and 30 minutes watching StreamerName!

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `[username]` (Optional): The username of the viewer whose watch time you want to check. If omitted, it defaults to the user issuing the command.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Loyalty system** to be active (`Loyalty` -> `Loyalty Settings`).
*   **Watch time tracking** must be enabled within the Loyalty Settings.
*   The command itself (`!watchtime`) is usually enabled by default when Loyalty is active.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!points`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/points)
    : Checks the loyalty points balance.
*   [`!top`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/top)
    : Shows the top viewers by watch time or points.
*   [`!leaderboard`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/leaderboard)
    : Provides a link to the full leaderboard.
*   [`!uptime`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/uptime)
    : Shows the duration of the _current_ stream session.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/watchtime#related-commands)

---

# !wrongsong | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#overview "Direct link to Overview")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!wrongsong` command allows viewers to remove the **last song they added** to the StreamElements media request queue. This is useful if you accidentally requested the wrong song or simply changed your mind.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#usage "Direct link to Usage")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To remove your last song request, simply type the command in chat:

    !wrongsong

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#examples "Direct link to Examples")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!wrongsong

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@ViewerName Removed your last song from the queue: Bohemian Rhapsody by Queen

example chat

ViewerName:!wrongsong

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@ViewerName You haven't requested any songs recently.

Parameters[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#parameters "Direct link to Parameters")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!wrongsong` command does not require any parameters.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Media Request** module to be enabled.
*   The command affects only the song requested by the user issuing the command.
*   Streamers can customize the response messages in the StreamElements dashboard under `Chatbot` -> `Chat Commands` -> `Default Commands`.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Used to add a song to the request queue.
*   [`!when`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when)
    : Checks the status of your last requested song.
*   [`!songqueue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue)
    : Provides a link to the full queue.
*   [`!song`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song)
    : Displays information about the currently playing song.
*   [`!next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/next)
    : Shows the next song in the queue.

Aliases[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#aliases "Direct link to Aliases")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Common default aliases may include:

*   `!ws`
*   `!removelast`

Streamers can configure additional aliases in the StreamElements dashboard.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#examples)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#parameters)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#related-commands)
    
*   [Aliases](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong#aliases)

# !when | StreamElements Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

On this page

Twitch

Overview[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#overview "Direct link to Overview")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `!when` command allows viewers to check the status of **their most recent song request** in the media request queue. It typically provides the song's position in the queue and an estimated time until it plays.

Usage[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#usage "Direct link to Usage")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To check the status of your last song request:

    !when

Examples[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#examples "Direct link to Examples")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example chat

ViewerName:!when

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, your song "The Best Song Ever" is at #4 in the queue and will play in approximately 12 minutes

example chat

ViewerName:!when

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, your song "Currently Playing" is at #1 in the queue and is playing right now

example chat

ViewerName:!when

![partner badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/d12a2e27-16f6-41d0-ab77-b780518f00a3/3 "partner")![moderator badge](https://static-cdn.jtvnw.net/badges/v1/3267646d-33f0-4b17-b3df-f923a41db1d0/3 "moderator")StreamElements:@User, you do not have a song in the queue.

Configuration[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires the **Media Request** module to be enabled.
*   The command checks the queue for a request made by the user issuing the command.
*   The response format (including estimated time) might be customizable in the Media Request module settings.

Related Commands[​](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#related-commands "Direct link to Related Commands")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`!songrequest`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songrequest)
    : Used to request a song.
*   [`!wrongsong`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/wrongsong)
    : Removes your last song request.
*   [`!songqueue`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/songqueue)
    : Provides a link to the full queue.
*   [`!song`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/song)
    : Shows the currently playing song.
*   [`!next`](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/next)
    : Shows the next song in the queue.

*   [Overview](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#overview)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#usage)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#examples)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#configuration)
    
*   [Related Commands](https://docs.streamelements.com/chatbot/commands/default/when#related-commands)
